### `[THE LARGEST CURATED ZSH COMPLETION CORPUS IN EXISTENCE // 28,339 FILES]`

> *"Every CLI you've heard of, completed. Plus several you haven't."*

> _"The shell is the street. The completions are the chrome."_

### [`strykelang`](https://github.com/MenkeTechnologies/strykelang) &middot; [`zshrs`](https://github.com/MenkeTechnologies/zshrs) · [`MenkeTechnologiesMeta`](https://github.com/MenkeTechnologies/MenkeTechnologiesMeta) · [`zpwr`](https://github.com/MenkeTechnologies/zpwr) · [`zshrs`](https://github.com/MenkeTechnologies/zshrs) · [`zsh-cargo-completion`](https://github.com/MenkeTechnologies/zsh-cargo-completion) · [`zsh-expand`](https://github.com/MenkeTechnologies/zsh-expand)

## [0x00] // WHAT IS THIS

A **massive** zsh completions plugin — over 28k command completions wired into compsys. Most were auto-generated by Python scripts that jacked into `--help` output, man pages, and web research, ripping completion data straight from the source. But then all completions have been cleaned, verified and updated with latest command options. Many have been handwritten as well.  Architecture-prefixed completions live in the `architecture_src` directory. A large ZUnit suite (see **// STATS** and **// TESTING**) validates structure, syntax, and coverage.

### // HARVESTED ECOSYSTEMS

Tool names for the completion corpus were harvested from:

- **Nix / nixpkgs** — every `pkgs.<attr>` shipping a binary
- **Homebrew** — every formula in `homebrew/core` (and the `cask` bottles that install CLIs)
- **Debian / Ubuntu APT** — every `bin/*` from `apt-cache pkgnames`, `/usr/share/man/man1`, `/usr/share/man/man8`, `/usr/share/man/man5`, `/usr/share/man/man6`, etc.
- **Fedora** — every binary from Fedora package repos
- **macOS system binaries** — `/usr/bin`, `/usr/sbin`, `/usr/libexec`, etc.
- **Kali Linux** — every binary shipped in the Kali package set
- **Alpine Linux** — `apk` package set
- **FreeBSD** — ports binaries and man pages
- **Various other Linux distros**
- **GitHub Releases** + **GitHub tree / code search** (multiple harvest rounds)
- **npm / npx / web research** — `create-*` scaffolders, scoped `@org/*` CLIs, and other Node tools verified against the npm registry (`npm view` bin/readme), live `npx … --help` output, package dist/tarballs, and upstream readmes (multi-round manual harvest; trivial or interactive-only scaffolders skipped)
- **Local zinit plugin checkouts** — completions vendored from installed plugins
- **crates.io**
- **Exotic language ecosystems** — Hackage (Haskell: `hakyll`, `shake`, `taffybar`), OPAM (OCaml: `odig`, `irmin`, `js_of_ocaml`, `learn-ocaml`, `alcotest`), Hex.pm (Elixir: `phx_new`, `ex_doc`, `dialyxir`, `igniter`, `mneme`), CPAN (Perl: `perlimports`, `perlnavigator`), CRAN (R: `radian`, `littler`), and AUR helpers (`aurman`, `pakku`) — verified against each project's cmdliner/argparse/OptionParser/Mix.Task switches, GetOptions definitions, or Cmd modules at the upstream source URL embedded in every completion file
- **Termux:API + Termux:tools** (Android) — all 57 `termux-*` commands from `termux-api-package/scripts/` (toast, vibrate, notification, sms-send, location, sensor, camera-photo, tts-speak, dialog, share, …) plus 13 `termux-*` commands from `termux-tools/scripts/` (backup, change-repo, info, open-url, reload-settings, restore, setup-storage, wake-lock, …) — flags parsed directly from each upstream `show_usage()` echo block and `getopts` spec, generated by `scripts/` automation
- **More exotic stragglers** — `nph` (Nim source formatter), `vab` (V Android Builder), `leo` (Aleo/Provable zero-knowledge language CLI), `cellranger` (10x Genomics single-cell sequencing pipeline) — flags from upstream README/usage docs / clap derive sources / 10x Cloud command-line argument reference
- **WebAssembly compiler toolchain** (Binaryen + WABT) — `wasm-as`, `wasm-dis`, `wasm-merge`, `wasm-shell`, `wasm-split`, `wasm-reduce`, `wasm-metadce`, `wasm-ctor-eval`, `wasm-fuzz-types`, `wasm-emscripten-finalize` (Binaryen, from `src/tools/*.cpp` + shared `ToolOptions` + 21-feature `feature.def`) and `wat-desugar` (WABT, from `src/tools/wat-desugar.cc`)
- **Bioinformatics** — `mash` (genome distance, marbl/Mash), `kraken2` + `kraken2-build` (taxonomic classification, DerrickWood), `centrifuge` + `centrifuge-build` + `centrifuge-inspect` (DaehwanKimLab), `trim_galore` (Rust rewrite — FelixKrueger), `macs2` (ChIP-seq peak caller — macs3-project/MACS, 138 flags across 12 subcommands), `deeptools` (NGS viz suite launcher) — verified against `GetOptions`, clap `cli.rs`, and argparse `add_argument` blocks
- **ML/AI tooling** — `llamafile` (Mozilla-Ocho, forwards llama.cpp common args), `vllm` (vllm-project, `entrypoints/cli/`), `wandb` (Click-based CLI), `mlflow` (Click-based CLI), `clearml` (multi-binary dispatch covering `clearml`, `clearml-session`, `clearml-serving`)
- **Astronomy, robotics, and misc** — `topcat` (Starlink/Bristol tabular data analyzer, SUN/253), `stilts` (TOPCAT's command-line companion, 50 tasks from SUN/256), `webots` (Cyberbotics robot simulator), `gazebo` + `gzserver` + `gzclient` (Gazebo Classic — new `gz` Ignition CLI deliberately not included; different architecture), `wllvm` + `wllvm++` + `extract-bc` (whole-program LLVM, travitch), `sox-ng` (modern SoX fork using `_ng` suffixed binaries), `pwn` (pwntools CTF/exploit-dev CLI, 20 subcommands from `pwnlib/commandline/main.py`)
- **Web3 / Blockchain** — `forc` (Sway/Fuel language, with plugin passthroughs to forc-fmt/forc-doc/forc-debug/forc-lsp/forc-publish/forc-tx), `btcwallet` (btcsuite Bitcoin wallet from `config.go` go-flags struct), `bcoin` + `bcoin-cli` + `bcoin-wallet` + `bwallet` + `bwallet-cli` (bcoin-org Bitcoin node + CLI), `movefmt` (Move language formatter, getopts-based), `move-prover` + `mvp` (Move formal prover, clap-derive from aptos-core)
- **TeX/LaTeX niche** — `latex2html` (113 Getopt::Long options), `mk4ht` (TeX4ht macro driver — 86 `<variant><dialect>` subcommands), `ltx2x` (LaTeX-to-XML/RTF/text), `latex-make` (CTAN make targets). `bibtexextract` deliberately skipped — no canonical tool exists by that name in CTAN or GitHub.
- **APL / Lisp / Smalltalk REPLs** — `gnu-apl` + `apl` (45 verified options from `UserPreferences.cc`), `klong` (kg.c usage), `kona` + `k` (kc.c args getopt), `ecl` (Embeddable Common-Lisp 30 options from cmdline.lsp), `pharo` (Pharo VM parameters from `parameters.c` + Smalltalk option handler)
- **Audio / EDA / Modern JS / Cargo** — `sonic-pi` + `sonic-pi-cli` (Widdershin/sonic-pi-cli `stop` subcommand only), `librepcb` + `librepcb-cli` (24 export options across open-project/library/symbol/package/step), `tjs` (txiki.js JS runtime: run/eval/serve/test/bundle/compile/app), `llrt` (AWS Low-Latency Runtime: compile/test), `cargo-dylint` (trailofbits Dylint clap structs), `cargo-features` (ToBinio cargo-features-manager `prune` subcommand)
- **Software-Defined Radio** — `rtl_433` (merbanan/rtl_433 — 38 options from src/rtl_433.c usage()), `hackrf-info` + `hackrf_info` (greatscottgadgets/hackrf — takes no flags upstream), `hackrf_sweep` (16 options + FFTW wisdom), `hackrf_clock` (HackRF Pro CLKIN/CLKOUT signal selection), `urh` + `urh_cli` (jopohl/urh Universal Radio Hacker — 37 cli flags for RX/TX/modulation/encoding), `sdrangel` + `sdrangelsrv` + `sdrangelbench` (f4exb/sdrangel MainParser flags), `sdrpp` (AlexandreRouma/SDRPlusPlus core/src/command_args.cpp defineAll())
- **Esoteric languages + live coding + niche cloud** — `lci` (justinmeza LOLCODE interpreter; main.c longopt table), `awib` (matslina Brainfuck compiler — no CLI flags, target via `@TARGET` directive in source), `foxdot` + `FoxDot` (Qirky/FoxDot Python live coding env for SuperCollider), `chicken` (Chicken Scheme compiler — 70+ flags from upstream wiki "Using the compiler" manual), `lakefs` (treeverse/lakeFS Git-for-data server — cobra subcommands run/setup/migrate/superuser/lua/gc/kv/flare, with nested migrate {version,up,goto,task} and kv {get,scan,dump,load})
- **Model Context Protocol server family** — All 7 active reference servers from `modelcontextprotocol/servers` (`mcp-server-everything` with stdio/sse/streamableHttp transports, `mcp-server-fetch` with `--user-agent`/`--ignore-robots-txt`/`--proxy-url`, `mcp-server-filesystem` with variadic allowed-directory paths, `mcp-server-git` with click `-r/--repository`/`-v/--verbose`, `mcp-server-memory`, `mcp-server-sequential-thinking`, `mcp-server-time` with `--local-timezone`) plus 11 archived servers from `modelcontextprotocol/servers-archived` still installable via `npx` (`mcp-server-{aws-kb-retrieval,brave-search,everart,gdrive,github,gitlab,google-maps,postgres,puppeteer,redis,slack}` — all are env-driven; only postgres/redis take a positional connection URL, only gdrive takes an optional `auth` token)
- **OCR + Modern AI/ML platforms** — `surya` family (`surya_ocr`, `surya_layout`, `surya_detect`, `surya_table`, `surya_latex_ocr`, `surya_gui`, `texify_gui` from datalab-to/surya), `marker` family (`marker`, `marker_single`, `marker_chunk_convert`, `marker_server`, `marker_gui`, `marker_extract` from datalab-to/marker), `nougat` + `nougat_api` (Meta Nougat scientific PDF OCR), `modal-client` (Modal serverless platform — 21 top-level + 53 nested subcommands), `marimo-cli` (Marimo reactive notebooks — 13 top-level subcommands), `cog-cli` (Replicate Cog ML packaging — 12 top-level subcommands), `e2b-cli` (E2B sandbox developer CLI — `auth`/`template`/`sandbox` groups with nested commands)
- **Linux / Bluetooth / AppImage / OIDC** — `appimage` + `*.AppImage` (meta-completion for AppImage runtime args from type2-runtime `runtime.c`), `appimaged` (probonopd/go-appimage daemon — `wrap`/`update`/`run`/`start` subcommands), `gattool` + `gatttool` (BlueZ legacy BLE attribute-protocol tool from bluez/attrib/gatttool.c), `iwspy` (wireless-tools spy list — positional-only grammar), `oidc-login` + `kubectl-oidc_login` (int128/kubelogin OIDC kubectl plugin — 23 flags across get-token/setup/clean)
- **ARM Cortex embedded toolchain** (`architecture_src/`) — all 20 `arm-none-eabi-*` cross-compiler + binutils binaries (`c++`, `g++`, `gcc`, `gcc-ar`, `gcc-nm`, `gcc-ranlib`, `addr2line`, `ar`, `as`, `c++filt`, `cpp`, `elfedit`, `ld`, `nm`, `objcopy`, `objdump`, `ranlib`, `readelf`, `size`, `strip`), mirrored from the existing `aarch64-linux-gnu-*` template family. `arm-none-eabi-gdb` was already covered by `more_src/_gdb-multiarch`'s multi-stem compdef.
- **VR/AR + IoT** — `monado-service` + `monado-cli` (Monado OpenXR runtime, test/probe subcommands; gitlab.freedesktop.org/monado), `openxr-explorer` + `openxrexplorer` (maluoi/openxr-explorer), `wivrn-server` + `wivrn-dashboard` (WiVRn streaming server — CLI11-based 9 flags), `mqtt-cli` + `mqtt` (HiveMQ MQTT CLI — 8 top-level subcommands + ~90 per-subcommand options from MqttCLICommand.java), `hass-cli` upgraded (Home Assistant CLI — full state-machine across 16 plugins)
- **Modern dev tools** — `mpy-cross` (MicroPython cross-compiler from mpy-cross/main.c), `cling` + `cling-jupyter` (C++ interactive interpreter — ClingOptions.td + clang passthroughs), `protoc-gen-ts` (TypeScript protoc plugin — stdin/stdout, no CLI; documented real OPTIONS keys in comment), `granted-cli` (common-fate Granted — urfave/cli 13 top-level subcommands), `aws-sso-cli` (synfinatic/aws-sso-cli — Kong-based 14 top-level subcommands)
- **3D printing + GIS** — `prusaslicer` + `prusa-slicer` (PrusaSlicer 42 CLI actions/transforms from PrintConfig.cpp; upgrade — old file was config-options-level), `cura-engine` + `CuraEngine` (Ultimaker CuraEngine slice/connect/help subcommands), `octoprint` (Click-based 11 top-level subcommands incl. serve/daemon/safemode/systeminfo/analysis/client/config/dev/plugins/timelapse/user), `qgis_process` (QGIS headless processing from qgsprocess.cpp), `grass8` + `grass` (GRASS GIS 8.x — `--tmp-project`/`--tmp-location`/`--tmp-mapset`/`--timeout`/`--config`), `grass7` (GRASS 7.x — `-wxpython`/`-wx`/`--wxpython`/`--wx`)
- **F# / .NET + Robotics** — `fake-cli` (FAKE F# Make build automation — Cli.fs docopt block), `paket-bootstrapper` + `paket.bootstrapper` (Paket bootstrapper from BootstrapperHelper.cs HelpText), `fsdocs` (F# docs generator — 4 verbs build/watch/init/convert, 37 flags across Option attributes), `fsx` + `fsxc` (F# script runner from nblockchain/fsx Fsxc.fs ParseArgsInternal), `rqt` (ROS Qt GUI framework — qt_gui_core/qt_gui/main.py argparse, 22 flags)
- **Cloud niche + Audio + Nix** — `upcloud-cli` + `upctl` (UpCloudLtd 21 top-level cobra subcommands + 104 nested), `exoscale-cli` (exoscale/cli 14 top-level subcommands, `_exo` already covers the actual binary), `fluidsynth` (FluidSynth real-time SoundFont synthesizer — 29 flags from src/fluidsynth.c long_options), `nix-direnv` + `nix-direnv-reload` (direnv stdlib extension — minimal CLI: only the generated `nix-direnv-reload` shim with no arguments). `hcloud-cli` deliberately skipped (Debian package name; binary is `hcloud`, already covered).
- **AI image/video upscaling (NCNN+Vulkan)** — `realsr-ncnn-vulkan` (Real-ESRGAN/Real-SR), `waifu2x-ncnn-vulkan`, `video2x` (k4yt3x — 42 flat flags via boost::program_options, not subcommands as spec assumed), `anime4kcpp` + `ac_cli` (Anime4KCPP — CLI rewrote to CLI11, has video subcommand)
- **Streaming + speech + media indexer** — `jacktrip` (Stanford CCRMA network audio — 59 flags from Settings.cpp longopts), `livekit-cli` + `lk` (LiveKit Cloud — 15 top-level cobra subcommands, ~50 nested), `livekit-egress` (LiveKit egress service), `rhvoice-test` + `rhvoice-service` + `RHVoice-test` + `RHVoice-service` (RHVoice speech synthesis), `moonlight-qt` + `Moonlight` (Moonlight Qt game-streaming client — 4 subcommands stream/list/pair/quit), `moonlight-embedded` + `moonlight` (Moonlight embedded — single-dash long options, 7 positional actions), `prowlarr` + `Prowlarr` (indexer aggregator — both `-flag` and `/flag` forms), `pavucontrol-qt` (Qt pavucontrol — QCommandLineOption block)
- **Hardware control + boot managers + Wi-Fi forensics + Wayland terminal IPC** — `ratbagctl` (libratbag gaming-mouse config — 8 top-level + nested actions), `poop` (Andrew Kelley's Performance Of Our Programs benchmark — 4 flags from src/main.zig), `zfsbootmenu` + `generate-zbm` (ZBM Boot Menu — 16 flags from bin/generate-zbm Perl Getopt::Long), `refind-install` + 4 sibling refind-* binaries (rEFInd EFI boot manager — refind-install/mkrlconf/mkdefault/mvrefind/mkfont per-binary dispatch), `hcxdumptool` + 8 sibling `hcx*tools` (Wi-Fi pcap/PMKID/handshake tools from ZerBea/hcxtools — `hcxpcapngtool` 31 flags / `hcxhashtool` 50 flags / etc.), `footclient` (foot Wayland terminal IPC client — 19 flags; agent fixed spec which incorrectly listed `foot-msg`)
- **Crypto wallet + PGP + QUIC stacks + game engine** — `trezorctl` (Trezor click-based CLI — 22 top-level subcommands + 10 globals), `sequoia-keystore` (Sequoia-PGP keystore daemon — clap derive, 7 flags), `ngtcp2-client` + `ngtcp2-server` (ngtcp2 reference QUIC implementation — 56/44 flags), `quicinterop` + `quicattack` (Microsoft msquic test tools — 12/8 flags), `quiche-client` + `quiche-server` (Cloudflare quiche QUIC — 39/30 flags from apps/src/args.rs ClientArgs/ServerArgs), `defold` (Defold game engine launcher — 67 flags + 5 subcommands build/bundle/clean/distclean/resolve from Bob.java; agent corrected spec which listed non-existent compile/run/update subcommands)
- **Bioinformatics + Astronomy (deep)** — `freebayes` (Bayesian variant caller — 79 long flags from src/Parameters.cpp long_options[]), `igv` (Integrative Genomics Viewer Java launcher), `sextractor` + `sex` + `source-extractor` (74 PARAM overrides from src/preflist.h), `scamp` (98 PARAM overrides), `swarp` + `SWarp` (64 PARAM overrides), `solve-field` (Astrometry.net solver wrapper — 92 long flags from solver/solve-field.c + augment-xylist.c), `astrometry-engine` (the actual Astrometry.net engine — 13 flags from solver/engine-main.c; agent corrected spec flags `-i/--input`/`-d/--inputs-dir`/`-s/--single`/`-r/--ranges` which don't exist upstream — real names are `--inputs-from`/`--base-dir`/`--solved`)
- **Hare language + OpenFOAM + DB + DNS** — `harec` (Hare compiler from sr.ht ~sircmpwn/harec — getopt string `"a:D:hM:m:N:o:Tt:v"`), `haredoc` (Hare doc extractor from ~sircmpwn/hare), `openfoam` + `openfoam-docker` + `openfoam-docker-arm` (OpenFOAM container wrapper — 26 flags), `pimpleFoam` (foamRun PIMPLE solver — argList common opts + `-solver`), `foamCleanCase` (OpenFOAM case-cleanup — 2 flags from bin/foamCleanCase usage()), `foamListTimes` (14 flags from foamListTimes.C addBoolOption + timeSelector::addOptions), `mssql-conf` (Microsoft SQL Server config — 8 subcommands setup/set/unset/traceflag/set-collation/set-edition/setup-ad-keytab/validate-ad-config + 36 settings), `aerospike-cli` (reugn/aerospike-cli SQL JDBC CLI — closest real binary by that exact name), `knot-dig` (Knot DNS dig alias — 139 entries: 16 `-` opts + ~123 `+[no]…` plus-options from kdig_params.c)
- **NCBI BLAST+ database utilities** — `blastdbcmd` (32 flags from c++/src/app/blastdb/blastdbcmd.cpp), `update_blastdb` + `update_blastdb.pl` (14 flags from update_blastdb.pl Getopt::Long table), `blastdb_aliastool` (24 flags incl. real `-oid_masks`/`-seqid_*` block), `blastdbcheck` (17 flags; spec's `-isam`/`-no_legacy`/`-binary_size` don't exist). Agent downloaded the NCBI BLAST+ 2.17.0 source tarball for verification.
- **HMMER 3.x utilities** — `hmmstat` (only `-h` upstream — spec's `--cpu`/`--mpi` aren't in ESL_OPTIONS), `hmmfetch` (5 flags incl. real `-O`), `hmmsim` (39 flags — full ESL_OPTIONS including `--mpi`/`--Eft`-family), `hmmemit` (15 flags incl. real `-C`/`-L`/`--local`/`--unilocal`/`--glocal`/`--uniglocal`/`--minl`/`--minu`), `hmmpgmd` (11 flags — spec's `--cs`/`--ws` don't exist, real is `--ccncts`/`--wcncts`), `hmmer` (no actual upstream binary — file written as documented placeholder for user-defined wrappers).
- **Voice / speech recognition + Arch build tools** — `whisper-cli` (whisper.cpp 66 flags from examples/cli/cli.cpp; legacy `main` upstream-deprecated, prints redirect warning to whisper-cli), `wyoming-piper` (rhasspy/wyoming-piper 20 flags incl. `--noise-w-scale`/`--noise-w` alias), `wyoming-faster-whisper` (21 flags). `wyoming-cli` deliberately skipped (rhasspy/wyoming is a protocol library with no console_scripts). `mkarchroot` (9 flags from src/mkarchroot.in getopts `'hUC:M:c:f:s'`; spec's `-N` doesn't exist), `makechrootpkg` (15 flags from src/makechrootpkg.in getopts; spec misclassified `-C` and bind flags — real semantics from upstream).

- **SiLK Round 3 — rwipfix2silk + rwsilk2ipfix + rwpmapbuild + rwpmapcat + rwpmaplookup + rwsiteinfo + rwswapbytes + rwtuc + rwsplit (9 binary stems via single multi-stem file, extends cumulative SiLK coverage to 26)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Flag inventory transcribed directly from upstream CERT NetSA per-tool docs at [tools.netsa.cert.org/silk/rwipfix2silk.html](https://tools.netsa.cert.org/silk/rwipfix2silk.html) + `rwsilk2ipfix.html`/`rwpmapbuild.html`/`rwpmapcat.html`/`rwpmaplookup.html`/`rwsiteinfo.html`/`rwswapbytes.html`/`rwtuc.html`/`rwsplit.html`. Single multi-stem file `_rwipfix2silk` is `#compdef rwipfix2silk rwsilk2ipfix rwpmapbuild rwpmapcat rwpmaplookup rwsiteinfo rwswapbytes rwtuc rwsplit`, dispatching on `$service` — covers the conversion + site-config + file-utility half of the SiLK suite. Combined with round-135 (`_rwfilter`, 8 stems) and round-136 (`_rwsetbuild`, 9 stems), **the repo now provides 26-stem SiLK coverage** which is essentially the full active toolkit. Shared `_meta` (5 flags) + `_disp` (8 flags) arrays carry over from round-136. **Per-stem coverage**: **`rwipfix2silk`** (IPFIX → SiLK binary): `--silk-output FILE`, `--interface-values snmp|vlan` (input/output interface meaning), `--log-destination none|stdout|stderr|PATH`, `--log-flags` (`sampling`/`show-templates`/`record-timestamps`), `--print-statistics`, repeatable `*--xargs FILE`. **`rwsilk2ipfix`** (SiLK → IPFIX): `--ipfix-output FILE`, `--single-template` (legacy single-template mode), `--no-site-name-elements` (exclude flowtype/class/type/sensor name elements), `--print-statistics`, `--site-config-file`. **`rwpmapbuild`** (text → binary prefix map): `--input-path FILE`/`--output-path *.pmap`, `--mode ipv4|ipv6|proto-port`, `--dry-run`, `--ignore-errors`, `--invocation-strip`. **`rwpmapcat`** (print prefix map contents): inherits `_disp` + **3-flag map-source mutex** `--map-file *.pmap` ↔ `--address-types[=FILE]` ↔ `--country-codes[=FILE]`, `--output-types` (comma-separated `_values -s ,` over `mapname`/`type`/`ranges`/`labels`), `--ignore-label`, `--ip-label-to-ignore IP`, `--no-cidr-blocks`, `--left-justify-labels`, deprecated `--integer-ips`/`--zero-pad-ips`. **`rwpmaplookup`** (lookup IPs against prefix maps): inherits `_disp` + same **3-flag map-source mutex** + **input-mode mutex** `--no-files` ↔ `--ipset-files`, repeatable `*--xargs`, `--fields` (comma-separated `_values -s ,` over `key`/`value`/`block`), `--no-errors`, deprecated IP-format flags. **`rwsiteinfo`** (silk.conf introspection): inherits `_disp` + `--fields` with a **17-value `_values -s ,` enum** seeded from the upstream field reference (`class`/`type`/`flowtype`/`sensor`/`sensor-id`/`sensor-description`/`default-class`/`default-type`/`repo-start-date`/`repo-end-date`/`file-size`/`group`/`default-class-type-list`/`class-type-list`/`class-list`/`sensor-list`/`flowtypes`), per-axis filters (`--classes`/`--types`/`--flowtypes`/`--sensors`/`--groups` — comma-separated), `--data-rootdir`/`--site-config-file`, `--timestamp-format`, `--list-delimiter` (for `:list` fields), `--help-fields`. **`rwswapbytes`** (byte-order conversion): **4-flag mutex** `--big-endian` ↔ `--little-endian` ↔ `--native-endian` ↔ `--swap-endian` (unconditional), 2 positionals (`infile`/`outfile`). **`rwtuc`** (text → SiLK uniform records): `--fields` (column parse spec), `--column-separator`, `--output-path`, `--bad-input-lines FILE` (capture unparseable lines), `*--xargs`, `--verbose`, `--stop-on-error`, `--no-titles`; **23 fixed-value override flags** for any field absent from text input (`--saddress`/`--daddress`/`--sport`/`--dport`/`--protocol`/`--packets`/`--bytes`/`--flags-all`/`--flags-initial`/`--flags-session`/`--stime`/`--etime`/`--duration`/`--sensor`/`--input-index`/`--output-index`/`--application`/`--class`/`--type`/`--icmp-type`/`--icmp-code`/`--attributes`/`--next-hop-ip` — the canonical pattern when text logs lack a field). **`rwsplit`** (split SiLK files by criteria): **4-flag split-criterion mutex** `--ip-limit N` ↔ `--flow-limit N` ↔ `--packet-limit N` ↔ `--byte-limit N`, `--basename PREFIX` (output filename prefix), random-sampling `--seed`/`--sample-ratio`/`--file-ratio`, `--max-outputs N`, `--print-filenames`, `--site-config-file`, repeatable `*--xargs`. **Blacklist additions (9)**: 4 inserted between `rwhod` (22769) and `rwsetbuild` (22770) for the `rwipfix2silk`/`rwpmap*` block; 2 between `rwsetunion` (22775) and `rwsnoop` (22776) for `rwsilk2ipfix`/`rwsiteinfo`; 1 between `rwsort` and `rwstats` for `rwsplit`; 2 between `rwstats` and `rwuniq` for `rwswapbytes`/`rwtuc`. Sort verified position-by-position: at index 2 'h' (104) < 'i' (105) < 'p' (112) < 's' (115) < 't' (116) < 'u' (117); within `rws*` at index 3 'e' < 'i' < 'n' < 'o' < 'p' < 't' < 'w'. LC_ALL=C sort verified.
- **SiLK Round 2 — rwsetbuild + rwsetcat + rwsetmember + rwsetintersect + rwsetunion + rwsettool + rwbagbuild + rwbagcat + rwbagtool (9 binary stems via single multi-stem file, extends round-135 SiLK coverage to 17)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Flag inventory transcribed directly from upstream CERT NetSA docs at [tools.netsa.cert.org/silk/rwsetbuild.html](https://tools.netsa.cert.org/silk/rwsetbuild.html) plus per-tool pages (`rwsetcat.html`/`rwsettool.html`/`rwbagbuild.html`/`rwbagcat.html`/`rwbagtool.html`). **Candidate-hunt dup-skip log this round (15 already-covered)**: LVM family `lvm`/`lvchange`/`lvcreate`/`lvremove`/`lvdisplay`/`lvs`/`vgcreate`/`vgremove`/`pvcreate`/`pvremove`/`pvs`/`vgs`/`lvconvert`/`lvextend`/`lvreduce` all at `man_src/_*` (a beautifully-comprehensive man-page-derived LVM corpus already in the repo). Single multi-stem file `_rwsetbuild` is `#compdef rwsetbuild rwsetcat rwsetmember rwsetintersect rwsetunion rwsettool rwbagbuild rwbagcat rwbagtool`, dispatching on `$service` — covers the IPset + Bag construction/manipulation half of the SiLK suite. The 9 tools share metadata + display flag sub-arrays. **Shared `_meta` array** (6 flags): `--note-add`/`--note-file-add`/`--invocation-strip` (header annotations), `--compression-method none|zlib|lzo1x|snappy|best`, `--help`/`--version`. **Shared `_disp` array** (8 flags, used in cat/display tools): `--output-path`, `--pager`, `--print-filenames`, `--no-columns`, `--column-separator`, `--no-final-delimiter`, `--delimited`, `--ip-format` (6-value enum: `canonical`/`decimal`/`hex`/`zero-padded`/`any-cidr`/`force-ipv6`). **Per-stem coverage**: **`rwsetbuild`** (text → IPset): `--ip-ranges[=DELIM]` (allow range pairs, default hyphen), `--record-version 0|2|3|4|5` (IPset format), positional `infile`/`outfile`. **`rwsetcat`** (print IPset contents): inherits `_disp`, plus `--count-ips`, `--print-ips`, `--print-statistics`, **3-flag mutex** `--cidr-blocks` ↔ `--ip-ranges` ↔ `--network-structure` (output style), deprecated `--integer-ips`/`--zero-pad-ips`. **`rwsetmember`** (test IPs against IPset): inherits `_disp`, `--count-records`, positionals 1=CIDR/IP pattern + repeatable IPset files. **`rwsetintersect`/`rwsetunion`** (thin wrappers — pre-set `rwsettool` mode): `--output-path`, `--record-version`, repeatable IPset inputs. **`rwsettool`** (general set arithmetic, 17 flags + 7-flag operation mutex): `--union` ↔ `--intersect` ↔ `--difference` ↔ `--symmetric-difference` ↔ `--sample` ↔ `--mask BLOCK-SIZE` ↔ `--fill-blocks BLOCK-SIZE`; sample modifiers `--size`/`--ratio 0.0..1.0`/`--seed`; output `--output-path`, `--modify-inplace` (atomic in-place via tmpfile), `--backup-path`, `--record-version`, `--note-strip`. **`rwbagbuild`** (text or IPset → Bag): `--set-input` ↔ `--bag-input` (2-flag input-source mutex), `--delimiter` (default `|`), `--proto-port-delimiter`, `--default-count`, **`--key-type` 12-value enum** (`sIPv4`/`dIPv4`/`sIPv6`/`dIPv6`/`sip-country`/`dip-country`/`sport`/`dport`/`protocol`/`stcpflags`/`dtcpflags`/`input`/`output`), **`--counter-type` 6-value enum** (`packets`/`bytes`/`records`/`sum-packets`/`sum-bytes`/`any-flag`), `--pmap-file MAPNAME:PATH`. **`rwbagcat`** (print Bag contents, ~14 flags): inherits `_disp` plus Bag-specific `--network-structure`, `--bin-ips` (invert: counter-bins by frequency), `--sort-counters increasing|decreasing`, range filters (`--minkey`/`--maxkey`/`--mincounter`/`--maxcounter`), `--mask-set FILE` (IPset filter), `--zero-counts` (include zero records), `--key-format` 7-value enum (`decimal`/`canonical`/`hex`/`zero-padded`/`timestamp`/`duration`/`epoch`), `--pmap-file`, `--print-statistics`, `--site-config-file`. **`rwbagtool`** (Bag arithmetic + filtering, 19 flags + 7-flag operation mutex): `--add` ↔ `--subtract` ↔ `--minimize` ↔ `--maximize` ↔ `--divide` ↔ `--scalar-multiply N` ↔ `--compare lt|le|eq|ge|gt`; masking `--intersect SETFILE`/`--complement-intersect SETFILE`, range filters (`--mincounter`/`--maxcounter`/`--minkey`/`--maxkey`), output transforms `--invert` (swap keys/counters), `--coverset` (output IPset instead of Bag) + `--ipset-record-version`, atomic write `--modify-inplace`/`--backup-path`, `--note-strip`. **Blacklist additions (9)**: 3 between `rwall` (22757) and `rwbypid.d` (22758) for the `rwbag*` block (`rwbagbuild`/`rwbagcat`/`rwbagtool`) and 6 between `rwhod` (22766) and `rwsnoop` (22767+) for the `rwset*` block (`rwsetbuild`/`rwsetcat`/`rwsetintersect`/`rwsetmember`/`rwsettool`/`rwsetunion`). Sort verified position-by-position: at index 2 the rw* block resolves as 'a' < 'b' < 'h' < 's'; within `rwbag*` at index 5 'b' (build) < 'c' (cat) < 't' (tool); within `rwset*` at index 5 'b' (build) < 'c' (cat) < 'i' (intersect) < 'm' (member) < 't' (tool) < 'u' (union); at index 3 `rwset*`'s 'e' (101) < `rwsnoop`'s 'n' (110). LC_ALL=C sort verified.
- **SiLK rw* family — rwfilter + rwstats + rwsort + rwuniq + rwcat + rwcount + rwfileinfo + rwgroup (8 binary stems via single multi-stem file)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-134 tightened `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Deferred: `dvdrip` truly fresh but it's a Perl-Tk GUI ripping/transcoding tool with no documented CLI surface beyond `dvd::rip --project FILE` — left for users who need it. Single multi-stem file `_rwfilter` is `#compdef rwfilter rwstats rwsort rwuniq rwcat rwcount rwfileinfo rwgroup`, dispatching on `$service` — covers CERT NetSA's flow-record analysis suite for IPFIX/NetFlow traffic. The 8 tools share an output framework but each has its own selection/aggregation surface. **Shared `_io` array** (14 flags re-applied per stem): `--output-path` (default stdout), repeatable `*--xargs FILE` (read filenames from file/stdin), `--print-filenames`, `--compression-method none|zlib|lzo1x|snappy|best`, `--note-add`/`--note-file-add` (annotate output header), `--site-config-file`, repeatable `*--plugin` (load C plugin), repeatable `*--pmap-file MAPNAME:PATH` (prefix maps for IP/port labels), repeatable `*--python-file *.py` (custom field code), `--temp-directory`, `--help`/`--version`/`--help-fields`. **Per-stem coverage**: **`rwfilter`** (~45 selection flags) — the workhorse query tool: time (`--start-date`/`--end-date YYYY/MM/DD[:HH]`, `--stime`/`--etime`/`--active-time`/`--duration`), repo (`--data-rootdir`, `--class`/`--type`/`--flowtypes`/`--sensors`), addresses (repeatable `*--scidr`/`*--dcidr`/`*--any-cidr` + `*--not-` negations, `*--saddress`/`*--daddress`/`*--any-address`, `*--sipset`/`*--dipset`/`*--anyset` for IPset-file lookups), ports/protos (`--sport`/`--dport`/`--aport`, `--protocol`, `--icmp-type`/`--icmp-code`), TCP flags (3-flag set `--flags-all`/`--flags-initial`/`--flags-session`), volume (`--bytes`/`--packets`/`--bytes-per-packet`), output partitioning (`--pass-destination`/`--fail-destination`/`--all-destination`), statistics (`--print-statistics`/`--print-volume-statistics`/`--max-pass-records`/`--max-fail-records`), advanced (`--tuple-file`/`--python-expr`/`--threads`/`--dry-run`). **`rwstats`** (Top-N/Bottom-N aggregation): `--fields`/`--values`, output limiting trio (`--count N`/`--threshold value`/`--percentage N`), **sort-direction mutex** `--top` ↔ `--bottom`, `--no-titles`/`--column-separator`. **`rwsort`**: `--fields` (sort keys), `--presorted-input` (merge-sort), `--reverse`, `--sort-buffer-size` (default ~2GB). **`rwuniq`** (binning + aggregation): `--fields`/`--values`/`--threshold FIELD=MIN[-MAX]`, time control (`--bin-time SEC`/`--nano-value-times`/`--timestamp-format`/`--epoch-time`), IP formatting (`--ip-format` 5-value enum `canonical`/`decimal`/`hex`/`any-cidr`/`force-ipv6`, `--integer-ips`/`--zero-pad-ips`), output format (`--no-titles`/`--no-columns`/`--column-separator`/`--delimited`). **`rwcat`** (concat + byte-order conversion): `--byte-order native|big|little`, `--ipv4-output`. **`rwcount`** (time-bin aggregation): `--bin-size SEC` (default 30), `--load-scheme` with 7-value enum (`start-time`/`end-time`/`middle`/`duration`/`time-proportional`/`minimum-volume`/`maximum-volume` — how to distribute multi-bin flows), `--start-time`/`--end-time`, `--skip-zeroes`. **`rwfileinfo`** (file-header introspection): `--fields`, `--summary`, `--no-titles`. **`rwgroup`** (flow grouping by key + delta): `--id-fields` (group keys), `--delta-field`/`--delta-value` (time-gap clustering), `--rec-threshold N`, `--objective`/`--summarize`. **Blacklist additions (8)**: all 8 rw* stems inserted into the `rw*` block — 5 between `rwbytype.d` and `rwho` (rwcat/rwcount/rwfileinfo/rwfilter/rwgroup) and 3 between `rwsnoop` and `rx` (rwsort/rwstats/rwuniq). Sort verified position-by-position: at index 2 the rw* block resolves as `b`<`c`<`f`<`g`<`h`<`s`<`u`; within the c-tied pair `rwcat`<`rwcount` (index 3 `a`<`o`); within the f-tied pair `rwfileinfo`<`rwfilter` (index 5 `e`<`t`); within the s-tied pair `rwsort`<`rwstats` (index 3 `o`<`t`). LC_ALL=C sort verified.
- **wodim (Debian's renamed cdrecord fork — CD/DVD-Recorder driver)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + an **upgraded round-116 grep using `^#compdef( |.* )${c}( |$)`** that tightens the word-boundary check per the round-133 false-positive lesson — `\<` was matching hyphenated containment like `pstops` inside `foo2zjs-pstops`; this round's pattern requires `pstops` to be either the first space-separated token after `#compdef ` or surrounded by spaces / end-of-line, eliminating the substring-in-hyphen-cluster failure mode). Flag inventory transcribed directly from upstream [manpages.debian.org/bookworm/wodim/wodim.1](https://manpages.debian.org/bookworm/wodim/wodim.1.en.html). **Candidate-hunt dup-skip log this round (substantial — 11 already-covered + 5 stock-zsh dups)**: `cdrecord` at `src/_cdrecord` + stock zsh (Joerg Schilling's original upstream — `wodim` is Debian's renamed fork following the 2006 licensing dispute), `mkisofs`/`cdda2wav` at `src/`, `flac`/`metaflac` at `more_src/` (plus stock `_flac`), `mosh`/`mosh-server` at `more_src/` (plus stock `_mosh`), `eternal-terminal`/`et` (the latter caught via multi-stem `more_src/_eternal-terminal` `#compdef` line — a clean example of the round-116 grep working as intended); stock-zsh dups `growisofs`/`cdrdao`/`abcde`/`abcde`. Single-file completion `_wodim` covers Debian's renamed `cdrecord` fork — the actual CD/DVD-burner workhorse on Debian/Ubuntu systems. ~70 flags across 8 functional groups: meta `-version`/`-checkdrive`/`-inq`/`-scanbus`/`--devices`/`-prcap`/`-atip`/`-toc`/`-msinfo` (all `(- *)` mutex — quit-after-print); verbosity stackable `*-v` (write progress) + `*-V` (SCSI transport; `-VV` shows buffer content); **device + tuning `key=value` syntax** (uncommon `value` completion via `+-`): `dev=` (via `_wodim_devs` helper running `wodim --devices` + awk-extraction of `dev=` lines for live device discovery), `speed=N`, `blank=` (5-mode enum `all`/`fast`/`track`/`session`/`unclose`), `fs=BYTES`, `minbuf=PCT` (25..95% ATAPI wait), `gracetime`/`timeout SEC`, `padsize`, `driver=NAME` (advanced manual selection), `driveropts=` (comma-separated with 6-value seed `burnfree`/`noburnfree`/`varirec`/`gigarec`/`audiomaster`/`forcespeed`), `cuefile=*.cue`/`msifile=`/`textfile=`. **Track-format 5-flag mutex** `-audio`/`-data`/`-mode2`/`-xa`/`-xa1` (CD-DA 44.1kHz vs CD-ROM mode 1 2048-byte sector vs mode 2 2336-byte vs XA mode 2 form 1 with drive-headers vs XA with app-headers). **Write-mode 7-flag mutex** `-tao`/`-sao`/`-dao`/`-raw`/`-raw96r`/`-raw96p`/`-raw16` (track-at-once default + session-at-once + DAO alias + the 4 raw subchannel variants). **Fixation mutex** `-fix` ↔ `-nofix`. Behavior `-multi` (multi-session), `-dummy` (laser-off dry-run — saves a coaster), `-eject`, `-load`/`-lock`, `-noclose`, `-force` (disable safety checks), `-immed` (non-blocking SCSI). **Padding mutex** `-pad` ↔ `-nopad`. `-isosize`, `-swab` (byte-swap little-endian audio for the drive), `-useinfo`, `-text` (write CD-Text from `.inf`/CUE). **Copy-protection 3-flag mutex** `-copy` (unrestricted) ↔ `-nocopy` (single-personal-copy default) ↔ `-scms` (no copying). Misc `-clone` (readom raw image), `-format` (CD-RW/DVD-RW/DVD+RW format). Trailing repeatable positional `*:track file:_files -g "*.(wav|cdr|raw|iso|cue|mp3|flac)"` covers the 7 common burn-source formats. `wodim` already in `blacklist.txt`; no add needed.
- **psutils Round 2 — pstops + psselect + epsffit + extractres + includeres (5 binary stems via single multi-stem file, completes psutils coverage to 9)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-116 `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Flag inventory transcribed directly from upstream [manpages.debian.org/bookworm/psutils/](https://manpages.debian.org/bookworm/psutils/) per-tool man pages (`pstops.1` + `psselect.1` + `epsffit.1` + `extractres.1` + `includeres.1`). **Tooling-bug callout discovered this round**: the round-116 `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep returned a **false positive** on `pstops` because the existing `src/_foo2zjs-pstops` file declares `#compdef foo2zjs-pstops` and the regex `^#compdef.*\<pstops\>` matches `pstops` as a word inside that hyphenated identifier (zsh-style `\<` word-boundary treats `-` as non-word). Verified by inspecting the actual `#compdef` line; `_foo2zjs-pstops` does NOT cover the bare `pstops` binary, so it remains truly fresh and is included in this round. Lesson for future grep upgrades: the word-boundary regex needs tightening (e.g. `^#compdef([^a-zA-Z0-9_-]|.* )pstops([^a-zA-Z0-9_-]|$)`) to reject hyphenated containment. **Candidate-hunt dup-skip log this round (5 already-covered)**: `psjoin` at `man_src/_psjoin`, `rootlesskit`/`slirp4netns`/`dvdauthor` all at `src/`, `enscript`/`genisoimage` ship in stock zsh at `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh/functions/`. Single multi-stem file `_pstops` is `#compdef pstops psselect epsffit extractres includeres`, dispatching on `$service` — companion to the round-132 `_psnup` multi-stem; **the two files together provide complete coverage of the 9 active psutils binaries** (psnup/psresize/psbook from round 132 + pstops/psselect/epsffit/extractres/includeres from this round + ps2pdf from round 132 as a Ghostscript wrapper). **`pstops`** (general page-by-page transform — the engine behind `psnup`'s n-up imposition): 6 flags + 3 positionals: `-q` (suppress page-number output), `-b` (prevent `bind` ops in PS prolog), `-w width`/`-h height`/`-p paper-name` (15-value enum from shared `_papers`), `-d lwidth` (draw border line, default 1pt); positionals 1 `page-spec` (e.g. `2:0(0,0)+1(0,0)` for the famous 2-up imposition spec), 2 `infile`, 3 `outfile`. **`psselect`** (page selector): 5 flags + 2 positionals: `-q`, **even/odd mutex** `-e` ↔ `-o`, `-r` (reverse output order), `-p pages` (e.g. `1,3-5,7` range expression). **`epsffit`** (EPS bounding-box fitter): 5 flags + 6 positionals: `-c` (centre image), `-r` (rotate 90° CCW), **aspect-vs-rotate mutex** `-a` (adjust aspect to fit, default preserve) ↔ `-m` (rotate-for-best-fit), `-s` (append `showpage` to force print); positionals 1..4 are the bounding-box coordinates `llx`/`lly`/`urx`/`ury` and 5..6 are `infile`/`outfile`. **`extractres`** (extract resources from a PostScript document): 1 flag `-m` (combine same-named resources into one file — needed for some font downloaders that emit fonts piece-by-piece). **`includeres`** (splice extracted resources back in): pure stdin → stdout filter with no documented flags — the completion returns `0` early so zsh just falls through to its default `_files` handling. All 5 stems already in `blacklist.txt`; no add needed.
- **PostScript transformation family — psnup + psresize + psbook + ps2pdf (4 binary stems via single multi-stem file)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-116 `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Flag inventory transcribed directly from upstream [manpages.debian.org/bookworm/psutils/](https://manpages.debian.org/bookworm/psutils/) (`psnup.1` + `psresize.1` + `psbook.1`) plus [manpages.debian.org/bookworm/ghostscript/ps2pdf.1](https://manpages.debian.org/bookworm/ghostscript/ps2pdf.1.en.html). **Candidate-hunt dup-skip log this round (7 already-covered)**: `ps2eps` at `src/_ps2eps`, `multipath`/`iscsiadm`/`iscsid`/`tgt-admin`/`tgtadm` all at `src/`/`man_src/`/`more_src/`. Single multi-stem file `_psnup` is `#compdef psnup psresize psbook ps2pdf`, dispatching on `$service` — covers Angus Duggan's 3 most-used PostScript-transformation tools from psutils plus the Ghostscript `ps2pdf` wrapper. **Shared paper-size enum** across `psnup`/`psresize` via `_papers` array (15 values: `a0`/`a1`/`a2`/`a3`/`a4`/`a5`/`b5`/`letter`/`legal`/`tabloid`/`statement`/`executive`/`folio`/`quarto`/`10x14` — the canonical psutils paper menu interpolated into `-p`/`-P` enum lists). **`psnup`** (n-up imposition, 16 flags + repeatable input) — output paper `-w width`/`-h height`/`-p paper-name`, input paper `-W width`/`-H height`/`-P paper-name`, **rotation 3-flag mutex** `-l` (landscape, 90° CCW) ↔ `-r` (seascape, 90° CW) ↔ `-f` (swap w/h without rotation), `-c` (column-major layout, default row-major), margins `-m margin` (around entire output) vs `-b border` (around each input page), `-d lwidth` (draw border line, default 1pt), `-s scale` (manual scale override), `-i nup` (pages per sheet — same as the unusual `-N` bare-number form per upstream), `-q` (suppress page-number output); positional `*:postscript file:_files -g "*.(ps|eps)"`. **`psresize`** (rescale + paper-format change, 7 flags + 2 positionals) — output `-w`/`-h`/`-p paper-name`, input `-W`/`-H`/`-P paper-name`, `-q`; positionals 1 `infile` and 2 `outfile`. **`psbook`** (signature reordering for bookbinding, 2 flags + 2 positionals) — `-q` (suppress page-number output), `-s N` (signature size — must be a multiple of 4; enum seeded with `4 8 12 16 20 24 28 32` covering the practical book-binding range). **`ps2pdf`** (GhostScript wrapper) — upstream man page explicitly defers to `gs(1)` for the full option set; this completion models the 9 most-practitioner-useful Ghostscript flags: `-dPDFSETTINGS=` with 5-preset enum (`/screen`/`/ebook`/`/printer`/`/prepress`/`/default` — the standard quality-vs-size trade-off menu used in 99% of ps2pdf invocations), `-dCompatibilityLevel=` with 7-version PDF enum (`1.2`/`1.3`/`1.4`/`1.5`/`1.6`/`1.7`/`2.0`), font controls `-dEmbedAllFonts=true|false`/`-dSubsetFonts=true|false`/`-dCompressFonts=true|false`, page handling `-dAutoRotatePages=/None|/All|/PageByPage`, image-resolution trio `-dColorImageResolution=dpi`/`-dGrayImageResolution=dpi`/`-dMonoImageResolution=dpi`; positionals 1 input `.ps`/`.eps` and 2 optional output `.pdf` (stdout if omitted). All 4 stems already in `blacklist.txt`; no add needed.
- **CUPS print-management family — lpstat + lpq + lprm + lpoptions + lpadmin (5 binary stems via single multi-stem file)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-116 `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Flag inventory transcribed directly from upstream Apple/OpenPrinting CUPS man pages at [www.cups.org/doc/man-lpstat.html](https://www.cups.org/doc/man-lpstat.html) + `man-lpq.html`/`man-lprm.html`/`man-lpoptions.html`/`man-lpadmin.html`. **Candidate-hunt dup-skip log this round (7 already-covered + 1 stock-zsh dup)**: `lp` ships in stock zsh at `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh/functions/_lp`, `lpc` already at `src/_lpc` (and multi-stem `src/_lpc.cups` `#compdef` line for the platform variant), `lpr` covered via multi-stem `src/_lpr-cups` `#compdef`; LaTeX-lint family `chktex`/`lacheck` at `src/`/`more_src/`; flow-analysis `cflow` at `more_src/`, `cscope` shipping stock zsh at `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh/functions/_cscope` (and `more_src/_cscope-indexer` multi-stem catches the wrapper variant). Single multi-stem file `_lpstat` is `#compdef lpstat lpq lprm lpoptions lpadmin`, dispatching on `$service` — covers the 5 user-facing CUPS print-management binaries. The family shares a common server-connection sub-set across all members: `-E` (force encryption to the CUPS server), `-h server[:port]` (alternate server via `_hosts`), `-U username` (alternate CUPS user via `_users`); beyond that each binary's flag set is distinct. **Live printer helper `_lp_printers`** runs `lpstat -p` and pipes through `awk '/^printer/ {print $2}'` to extract installed printer names for the `-d`/`-p`/`-P`/`-o`/`-v`/`-x` printer-target positionals — works against the local CUPS instance by default but follows `-h`/`-U` overrides via env propagation. **Per-stem coverage**: **`lpstat`** (18 flags) — print-system introspection covering jobs (`-o destination`, `-u user`, `-W completed|not-completed`, `-R` ranking), printers (`-p`/`-a`/`-v`/`-c`/`-l` long-listing), defaults (`-d`/`-e`/`-r` server-running/`-s` summary/`-t` everything), connection (`-E`/`-H`/`-h`/`-U`); **`lpq`** (8 flags) — queue status with `-P printer`, `-a` (all printers), `-l` (long format), trailing `+interval` continuous-polling syntax (e.g. `lpq +5` to refresh every 5 seconds), positional `*:job-id:`; **`lprm`** (6 flags) — job cancellation with `-P printer`, bare `-` (cancel all queued jobs), positional `*:job-id:` for selective removal; **`lpoptions`** (8 flags) — per-user option editing with `-d destination[/instance]` (set user default), `-p destination[/instance]` (set instance context), `-l` (list current options), repeatable `*-o name[=value]` (set option), `-r option` (remove option), `-x destination[/instance]` (clear all instance options); **`lpadmin`** (17 flags) — administrator-only printer setup with `-p destination` (configure named printer), `-x destination` (delete), `-c class`/`-r class` (class membership add/remove), `-d destination` (system default), `-v device-uri` (queue backend), `-m model` (PPD model), `-D info`/`-L location` (textual metadata), `-u expr` (user-level access policy), repeatable `*-o name=value` (PPD/job options) + repeatable `*-R name-default` (delete defaults), deprecated `-i FILE` (interface script) / `-P FILE` (`.ppd` glob). All 5 stems already in `blacklist.txt`; no add needed.

The `generate clusterconfig` leaf covers `-p/--provider` with the full 6-provider enum (`vsphere`/`tinkerbell`/`docker`/`snow`/`cloudstack`/`nutanix`) + cluster-name positional. **`exp` state machine** (experimental subcommands): 2-target enum (`validate`/`vsphere`). Remaining subcommands (`get`/`describe`/`list`/`install`/`import`/`apply`/`renew`/`check-images`/`copy`/`download`) fall through to generic positional handling — they have their own per-target sub-trees that need more docs to source-verify; deferred for a future round. `eksctl-anywhere` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 7151 between `eksctl` (7150) and `elan` (7151 → 7152) — sort verified shared `eksctl` prefix means `eksctl` (length 6) < `eksctl-anywhere` (length 15) by shorter-string-wins; at index 1 `eksctl-anywhere`'s 'k' (107) < `elan`'s 'l' (108). - **otfcc family — otfccdump + otfccbuild (Caryll Studio's OpenType compiler/decompiler, 2 binary stems via single multi-stem file)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-116 `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Flag inventory transcribed directly from upstream [github.com/caryll/otfcc](https://github.com/caryll/otfcc) README options table. **Candidate-hunt dup-skip log this round (8 already-covered)**: `fc-list`/`fc-cache`/`fc-match` at `src/`, `mkfontscale` at `man_src/`, `pyftsubset` at `more_src/` (with multi-stem in `src/_pyftsubset`'s `#compdef`), `xmllint`/`xsltproc` at `src/`. Single multi-stem file `_otfccdump` is `#compdef otfccdump otfccbuild`, dispatching on `$service` — covers Caryll's bidirectional OpenType font compiler used heavily in font-engineering workflows where you decompile binary OTF/TTF → JSON, patch font tables, then recompile JSON → OTF/TTF. **`otfccdump`** (decompile → JSON, 14 flags): meta `-h/--help`, `-v/--version`; output `-o FILE` (defaults to stdout, JSON glob); TTC sub-font selection `-n/--ttc-index N`; **JSON formatting mutex** `--pretty` ↔ `--ugly`; `--verbose`; content filters `--ignore-glyph-order`, `--glyph-name-prefix pfx`, `--ignore-hints`, `--decimal-cmap` (`cmap` keys as decimal numbers vs default hex), `--name-by-hash`; **BOM mutex** `--add-bom` ↔ `--no-bom`; input via `_files -g "*.(otf|ttf|ttc|otc)"` covering all 4 OpenType container forms. **`otfccbuild`** (compile JSON → OTF/TTF, 24 flags + 4-level optimization enum): meta `-h/--help`, `-v/--version`; output `-o FILE`; **4-level optimization mutex** `-O0` (off) ↔ `-O1` (default) ↔ `-O2` (aggressive web-font) ↔ `-O3` (most aggressive); `-s/--dummy-dsig` (empty DSIG table — needed for self-signing some Windows scenarios), `--verbose`, `--ignore-hints`; **preservation flags** `--keep-average-char-width` (preserve `OS/2.xAvgCharWidth`), `--keep-unicode-ranges` (preserve `OS/2.ulUnicodeRange`), `--keep-modified-time` (keep `head.modified` from JSON), `--short-post` (no glyph names in output); **glyph-order 3-flag mutex** `-i/--ignore-glyph-order` ↔ `-k/--keep-glyph-order` ↔ `--dont-ignore-glyph-order` (the last is an explicit alias for `--keep-glyph-order` — encoded so users get tab discovery of both spellings); **feature dedup mutex** `--merge-features` ↔ `--dont-merge-features`; **lookup dedup mutex** `--merge-lookups` ↔ `--dont-merge-lookups`; CFF-table tweaks `--force-cid` (name-keyed → CID-keyed conversion), `--subroutinize` (CFF table subroutinization for size); cmap `--stub-cmap4` (stub `cmap` format 4 subtable when format 12 is present, for legacy-tool compat); input via `_files -g "*.json"`. **Blacklist additions (2)**: `otfccbuild` and `otfccdump` inserted between `oterm` (18537) and `otfinfo` (18538) — sort verified at index 3 `otfcc*`'s 'c' (99) < `otfinfo`'s 'i' (105); - **dolphin-tool (Dolphin emulator's headless companion CLI — Wii/GameCube disc image toolkit)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-116 `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Subcommand inventory + per-leaf flag detail extracted from upstream `Source/Core/DolphinTool/{Command,ConvertCommand,VerifyCommand,HeaderCommand,ExtractCommand}.cpp` on [dolphin-emu/dolphin](https://github.com/dolphin-emu/dolphin). **Candidate-hunt dup-skip log this round (8 already-covered)**: `mednafen`/`mame`/`dolphin-emu`/`pcsx2`/`ppsspp`/`scummvm` all at `more_src/_*`; `browsh`/`nyxt` at `more_src/`. **Note on `duckstation`** truly fresh but upstream doesn't ship an official headless `duckstation-cli` binary — the `duckstation-qt`/`duckstation-nogui` flavours are GUI-launchers with `-batch` startup mode but no proper subcommand CLI; skipped per the "no rich CLI surface" precedent. Single-file completion `_dolphin-tool` covers the Wii/GameCube disc image toolkit shipped alongside the Dolphin emulator for headless format conversion + verification + extraction workflows (common in archival ROM-hacking pipelines). 4 subcommands via `_subcmds` describe: `convert` (transform between ISO/GCZ/WIA/RVZ + optional scrub + compress), `verify` (validate integrity + compute CRC32/MD5/SHA1/rchash digests), `header` (dump metadata: block size, compression details), `extract` (unpack files/partitions). **`convert`** (9 flags): `-u/--user DIR` (Dolphin user folder, auto-created), `-i/--input FILE`, `-o/--output FILE`, `-f/--format` (4-value enum `iso\|gcz\|wia\|rvz`, default `rvz`), `-s/--scrub` (junk-data scrubbing), `-b/--block_size N` (RVZ default `131072` = 128 KiB), `-c/--compression` (5-value enum `none\|zstd\|bzip2\|lzma\|lzma2`, RVZ default `zstd`), `-l/--compression_level N` (RVZ zstd default 5). **`verify`** (4 flags): `-u/--user`, `-i/--input`, `-a/--algorithm` (4-value enum `crc32\|md5\|sha1\|rchash`). **`header`** (6 flags): `-i/--input`, `-j/--json` (machine-readable; overrides individual print flags), `-b/--block_size`, `-c/--compression`, `-l/--compression_level` (each as a boolean toggle for selective display). **`extract`** (8 flags): `-i/--input`, `-o/--output DIR`, `-p/--partition PARTITION`, `-s/--single PATH` (single-file/directory mode), `-l/--list` (list contents, honours `--single`), `-q/--quiet`, `-g/--gameonly` (DATA partition only). Input file completion across all subcommands uses `_files -g "*.(iso|gcz|wia|rvz|wbfs|ciso)"` covering the 6 common Wii/GameCube container formats (ISO baseline, GCZ Dolphin-native, WIA WiiTime archive, RVZ Dolphin-next-gen, WBFS USB-loader, CISO Compressed-ISO). `dolphin-tool` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 6542 between `dolphin-emu` and `dolphin5` (sort verified position-by-position: at index 8 `dolphin-emu`'s 'e' (101) < `dolphin-tool`'s 't' (116); at index 7 `dolphin-tool`'s '-' (45) < `dolphin5`'s '5' (53)). LC_ALL=C sort verified.

Single-file completion `_pacseek` covers the interactive TUI for searching and installing Arch Linux packages — most navigation is keyboard-driven inside the TUI (ENTER/TAB/CTRL+S settings/CTRL+Q quit), config persisted at `~/.config/pacseek/config.json`, so the CLI surface is intentionally thin. 7 flags: meta `-h/--help`; repo filtering `-r REPOS` (comma-separated list, completes via `_values -s ,` with a static seed of 10 common Arch repos — `core`/`extra`/`multilib` + their `-testing` variants, plus `aur`/`chaotic-aur`/`eos`/`endeavouros-aur` for derivative-distro users); initial state `-s TERM` (initial search term), `-u` (show upgrades after startup), `-i` (show installed packages after startup); rendering `-a` (ASCII mode — no Unicode box-drawing, useful for serial consoles + Windows Terminal pre-fluent builds), `-m` (monochrome mode — no colours, useful for tmux-pipes / `script` recordings). - **FRR daemon family expansion — pbrd + ripngd (2 binary stems via single multi-stem file, fills out the FRR routing-daemon coverage to 11)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-116 `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Common-flag inventory transcribed directly from upstream [docs.frrouting.org/en/latest/basic.html](https://docs.frrouting.org/en/latest/basic.html) plus per-daemon pages: [pbr.html](https://docs.frrouting.org/en/latest/pbr.html) and [ripngd.html](https://docs.frrouting.org/en/latest/ripngd.html) (both daemons explicitly defer to the common-options page — they ship no daemon-specific invocation flags). **Candidate-hunt dup-skip log this round (9 FRR daemons already-covered)**: `babeld`, `bgpd`, `eigrpd`, `isisd`, `ldpd`, `nhrpd`, `ospf6d`, `ospfd`, `pimd`, `ripd`, `staticd` — all already at `more_src/_*` (a remarkably-comprehensive FRR coverage already in the repo; this round just fills in the last 2 missing daemons). Single multi-stem file `_pbrd` is `#compdef pbrd ripngd`, dispatching on `$service` — both daemons share the FRR-common command-line flag set verbatim (per upstream both pages explicitly say "There are no $daemon-specific invocation options. Common options can be specified"). `pbrd` is FRR's Policy-Based Routing daemon (per-source/per-application routing decisions beyond destination-only matching); `ripngd` is FRR's RIPng (RIP for IPv6) routing daemon, the IPv6 sibling of `ripd`. **18 shared flags** (the FRR common-invocation set): meta `-h/--help`, `-v/--version`; daemonize `-d/--daemon`; config `-f/--config_file FILE`, `-i/--pid_file FILE`, `-z/--socket FILE` (zebra control socket); VTY `-A/--vty_addr ADDR`, `-P/--vty_port PORT`; identity `-u/--user USER` (via `_users`), `-g/--group GROUP` (via `_groups`); namespacing `-N/--pathspace NS` (per-instance config namespace), `-w/--vrfwnetns` (discover VRFs via Linux network namespaces — Linux-only feature), `-o/--vrfdefaultname NAME` (override "Default VRF" CLI display name); module loading `-M/--module module[:opts]` (FRR's pluggable module system — used for SNMP, etc); logging `--command-log-always` (permanent command logging), `--log dest` (initial destination — special `(stdout syslog)` enum plus `file:/path` form via `_alternative`), `--log-level` with 8-value enum (`emergencies`/`alerts`/`critical`/`errors`/`warnings`/`notifications`/`informational`/`debugging`); CLI features `--tcli` (transactional CLI mode); resource limits `--limit-fds N`. The `--log` flag uses `_alternative` to multiplex two surfaces — the bare special values `stdout`/`syslog` and the `file:/path` form via `_files` — matching upstream's `--log <stdout|syslog|file:/path/to/log/file>` syntax. **Blacklist additions (2)**: `pbrd` inserted between `pbr` (19043) and `pbs_iff` (19044) — sort verified shared `pbr` prefix means `pbr` (length 3) < `pbrd` (length 4) by shorter-string-wins, and `pbrd`'s `r` (114) < `pbs_iff`'s `s` (115) at index 2; `ripngd` inserted between `ripmime` (22257) and `rippkgs` (22258) — sort verified at index 3 `ripmime`'s 'm' (109) < `ripngd`'s 'n' (110) < `rippkgs`'s 'p' (112). - **rmlint (Christopher Pahl & Daniel Thomas's duplicate-and-lint finder)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-116 `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Flag inventory transcribed directly from upstream [manpages.debian.org/bookworm/rmlint/rmlint.1](https://manpages.debian.org/bookworm/rmlint/rmlint.1.en.html). **Candidate-hunt dup-skip log this round (8 already-covered)**: round-124's deferred mkvtoolnix CLI family — `mkvmerge`/`mkvinfo`/`mkvextract`/`mkvpropedit` — all turned out to **already be covered** at individual `more_src/_mkv*` files (the earlier deferral was based on an incorrect "deferred for multi-stem fanout" call; the per-tool completions were already shipped). Round-124's `daemontools` deferral also resolved: `svc`/`svstat`/`svscan`/`supervise` all at `more_src/` (some catching via `_s6-svstat`/`_s6-svscan` multi-stem `#compdef` lines), plus `jdupes` at `more_src/_jdupes` and `exiv2` at `src/_exiv2`. Single-file completion `_rmlint` covers the duplicate-and-lint finder — locates duplicate files, empty files/dirs, broken symlinks, broken sUid/sGid bits, non-stripped binaries, and bad encodings; outputs a shell script that can be reviewed before running to actually delete the cruft (the "review-before-delete" workflow is rmlint's killer feature for safe dedup). ~58 flags grouped with 14 mutex sets: meta `-h/--help`, `-H/--show-man` (open full manpage), `--version` (shows compiled-feature list). **Output**: repeatable `*-T/--types` (CSV `+/-name` filter — e.g. `+duplicates,-emptyfiles`), repeatable `*-o/--output fmt:file` (custom format-to-file pairs), repeatable `*-O/--add-output fmt:file` (add without overwriting defaults), repeatable `*-c/--config key=value` (formatter knob). **Filters**: `-z/--perms RWX` (permission filter), `-s/--size RANGE` (e.g. `1K-100M`), `-d/--max-depth N`. **Hash algorithm enum (`-a/--algorithm`)** with 24 values covering the full upstream menu: blake2b/blake2bp/blake2s/blake2sp, sha3 family, sha256/sha512/sha1/md5, highway64/128/256, metro/metro256/metrocrc/metrocrc256, xxhash, murmur/murmur256, city/city256, cumulative, ext, paranoid. **Paranoia mutex** `-p/--paranoid` ↔ `-P/--less-paranoid`. **Verbosity mutex** stackable `-v/--loud` ↔ `-V/--quiet`. **Progress mutex** `-g/--progress` ↔ `-G/--no-progress`. **Color mutex** `-w/--with-color` ↔ `-W/--no-with-color`. **Hardlink mutex (3-flag)** `-l/--hardlinked` ↔ `-L/--no-hardlinked` + `--keep-hardlinked`. **Symlink mutex (3-flag exclusion)** `-f/--followlinks` ↔ `-F/--no-followlinks` ↔ `-@/--see-symlinks` (the last is rmlint's `@` trick: a single character flag, encoded literally so zsh doesn't choke on the `@`). **Crossdev mutex** `-x/--no-crossdev` ↔ `-X/--crossdev`. **Hidden mutex** `-r/--hidden` ↔ `-R/--no-hidden` + `--partial-hidden`. **Basename matching mutex** `-b/--match-basename` ↔ `-B/--unmatched-basename`. **Extension matching pair-mutex** `-e/--match-with-extension` ↔ `-E/--no-match-with-extension`, plus `-i/--match-without-extension` ↔ `-I/--no-match-without-extension`. **Time filtering**: `-n/--newer-than-stamp FILE` vs `-N/--newer-than TIME`. **Tagged-path semantics**: `-k/--keep-all-tagged` (preserve tagged), `-K/--keep-all-untagged` (preserve untagged), `-m/--must-match-tagged` (only dups in tagged), `-M/--must-match-untagged` (only dups in untagged), `-S/--rank-by` with 20-value enum (`m`/`a`/`c`/`M`/`A`/`C`/`l`/`L`/`p`/`P`/`x`/`X`/`h`/`H`/`o`/`O`/`d`/`D`/`r`/`R`). **Replay mode** `--replay FILE` (reprocess previous JSON output with new filters — the rmlint workflow lets you tweak filtering without re-hashing). **xattr caching** `-C/--xattr` (cache to xattrs) + sub-flags `--xattr-read`/`--xattr-write`/`--xattr-clear`. **Misc**: `-U/--write-unfinished`, `-t/--threads N`, `-u/--limit-mem SIZE`, `-q/--clamp-low N` and `-Q/--clamp-top N` (examine only a portion of each file from start/end — useful for fast video-prefix matching), `-Z/--mtime-window SECONDS`, `--with-fiemap`/`--without-fiemap`. Repeatable trailing positional `*:path:_files -/`. `rmlint` already in `blacklist.txt` at line 22312; no add needed.
- **sleepenh (Edrusb's high-precision drift-correcting sleep)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-116 `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Single-file completion `_sleepenh` covers the high-precision drift-correcting sleep utility — unlike `sleep(1)` which sleeps for a fixed duration, `sleepenh` aligns its wakeup to an absolute timestamp so chained invocations don't accumulate drift, ideal for periodic-task loops where you want exactly N seconds between wakes regardless of how long the work in between took. 3 flags + 2 positionals: meta `-h/--help`, `-V/--version`; `-w/--warp` (adjust returned timestamp so the next sleepenh call is guaranteed to actually sleep — useful when the previous iteration's work overran the budget); positional 1 `INITIALTIME` (defaults to now if omitted), positional 2 `TIMETOSLEEP` (seconds — the canonical use is `T=$(sleepenh $T 1.5)` in a Bash loop to maintain a 1.5-second period). `sleepenh` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 23780 between `sleep` and `slic3r` (sort verified position-by-position: shared `sleep` prefix means `sleep` (length 5) < `sleepenh` (length 8) by shorter-string-wins; at index 2 `sleepenh`'s 'e' (101) < `slic3r`'s 'i' (105)). LC_ALL=C sort verified.

Output: `-o FILE`, `-format` with 22-format enum (`msh`/`msh1`/`msh2`/`msh4`/`stl`/`vrml`/`unv`/`vtk`/`wrl`/`mesh`/`ply`/`ply2`/`bdf`/`cgns`/`med`/`inp`/`diff`/`key`/`x3d`/`ir3`/`mail`/`neu`/`su2`/`p3d`), `-bin` (binary when available), `-saveall` (discard physical groups). Display: `-n` (hide meshes/views on startup), `-fontsize`, `-display`. File ops: `-new` (new model before merge), `-merge`/`-open` (next files), `-pid` (PID to stdout), `-listen SOCKET`. Verbosity `-v 0..5,99` (99 = full debug). Scripting: `-nopopup`, repeatable `*-setnumber name value`, `*-setstring name value`, `*-string option`, `*-option FILE` (parse option file). Post-processing: `-combine` (merge views into multi-time-step). Batch convert: `-convert files` (latest formats + exit). Flag inventory transcribed directly from upstream [manpages.debian.org/bookworm/likwid/likwid-topology.1](https://manpages.debian.org/bookworm/likwid/likwid-topology.1.en.html) + `likwid-perfctr.1` + `likwid-pin.1` + `likwid-powermeter.1` + `likwid-mpirun.1` + `likwid-setFrequencies.1` (6 source-verified members; `features` and `genTopoCfg` covered as stubs since their man pages were not source-verified this round). Single multi-stem file `_likwid-topology` is `#compdef likwid-topology likwid-perfctr likwid-pin likwid-powermeter likwid-mpirun likwid-setFrequencies likwid-features likwid-genTopoCfg`, dispatching on `$service` — covers RRZE-HPC's performance toolkit for x86/ARM/POWER multi-core systems (the LIKWID = "Like I Knew What I'm Doing" tooling that's a staple of academic HPC perf work). The family shares a common short-flag style across all members: `-c cpu-list` (CPU expression — e.g. `0,1,2` or `0-7` or `S0:0-7@S1:8-15`), `-V`/`--verbose` level (0..3), `-v`/`--version`, `-h`/`--help`. **`likwid-topology`** (CPU/cache/NUMA introspection, 8 flags): `-g` ASCII-art topology (no GPU), `-c/--caches` detailed cache hierarchy, `-C/--clock` measure processor clock, `-G/--gpus` Nvidia GPU info, `-o/--output FILE` with suffix-driven filter (`.csv`/`.xml`/`.json` automatic). **`likwid-perfctr`** (hardware counter measurement, 22 flags + trailing command): mode switches `-m/--marker` (marker-API mode), `-a` (list available perf groups + exit), `-e` (list available counters + events + exit), `-H` (group-help with `-g`), `-i/--info` (cpuid + Intel PMU detail), `--stats` (always print stats table); selection `-c cpu-expr` vs `-C cpu-expr` (latter pins threads), `-g/--group GROUP`, `-G/--gpus gpu-list` + `-W/--gpugroup`, `-E search-str` (filter events by substring); modes `-t freq` (timeline), `-S waittime` (end-to-end via sleep), `-T time` (group-switch interval); output `-o/--output FILE`, `-O` (CSV); plumbing `-s/--skip hex-mask`, `-f/--force` (force register writes); trailing `*:::command:_command_names -e` for the wrapped process. **`likwid-pin`** (NUMA pinning launcher, 11 flags + trailing command): selection `-c`/`-C cpu-expr`, `-p` (print thread domains), `-d delim` (CPU delimiter); NUMA policy mutex `-i` (interleave) ↔ `-m` (membind); cleanup `-S/--sweep` (clean ccNUMA domains pre-run); `-s/--skip hex-mask`, `-q/--quiet`; trailing `*:::command:_command_names -e`. **`likwid-powermeter`** (RAPL-based power + temp readout, 10 flags): `-c socket-list`, `-M 0|1` (MSR access mode — 0=direct, 1=accessDaemon), `-s duration` (units `us`/`ms`/`s`), `-p` (dynamic clocks + CPI per socket), `-i/--info` (TDP + Turbo steps per RAPL domain), temperature mutex `-t` (Celsius) ↔ `-f` (Fahrenheit). **`likwid-mpirun`** (MPI launcher with pinning + counters, 14 flags + trailing command): MPI plumbing `-n`/`-np`/`--n`/`--np N` (4-way alias), `-hostfile FILE`, `-nperdomain N`, `-pin EXPR`, `-mpi intelmpi|openmpi|slurm|mvapich2` (4-value enum), `-omp intel|gnu` (hybrid OMP runtime); marker mode `-m/--marker`; output `-O` (CSV); passthrough `--mpiopts opts`; `-d/--debug`, `-s/--skip hex-mask`, trailing `*:::command:_command_names -e`. **`likwid-setFrequencies`** (CPU governor + freq control, 14 flags): info `-p` (current freqs), `-l` (configurable freqs), `-m` (configurable governors); apply `-c cpu-list`, `-g governor` (6-value enum: `performance`/`powersave`/`ondemand`/`conservative`/`schedutil`/`userspace`), `-f/--freq`, `-x/--min`/`-y/--max` constraints, `-t/--turbo 0|1`; Intel-only Uncore `--umin`/`--umax`, `--reset` (defaults + performance governor), `--ureset` (reset Uncore to max). **`likwid-features`/`likwid-genTopoCfg`** stub coverage (common short-flag conventions; man pages not source-verified this round so only the universal `-h`/`-v`/`-V`/`-c`/`-o` are modeled). **Blacklist additions (8)**: all 8 likwid stems inserted between `ligolo-proxy` (13785) and `lilo` (13786) in upstream-canonical order: `likwid-features` (f=102) < `likwid-genTopoCfg` (g=103) < `likwid-mpirun` (m=109) < `likwid-perfctr` (p,e=112,101) < `likwid-pin` (p,i=112,105) < `likwid-powermeter` (p,o=112,111) < `likwid-setFrequencies` (s=115) < `likwid-topology` (t=116). Sort verified position-by-position: at index 2 `ligolo`'s 'g' (103) < `likwid`'s 'k' (107) < `lilo`'s 'l' (108); within the `likwid-*` block, suffix order resolves correctly per the index-7+ table above. LC_ALL=C sort verified.

Single-file completion `_bsdtar` covers libarchive's tar implementation — the default `tar` on macOS and FreeBSD; reads/writes 12+ archive formats (ustar/pax/cpio/zip/iso9660/ar/7zip/xar/mtree/etc) plus all the compression variants (gzip/bzip2/xz/compress/lzma/lzop/lrzip/lz4/zstd). ~80 flags grouped: 5-flag **mode mutex** (`-c`/`-x`/`-t`/`-r`/`-u`); 10-flag **compression mutex** (the 9 `-z`/`-j`/`-J`/`-Z`/`--lzma`/`--lzop`/`--lrzip`/`--lz4`/`--zstd` + auto-detect `-a/--auto-compress` — all exclude each other via a single shared `(-z --gzip ...)` zsh exclusion list); archive io `-f/--file` (- for stdin/stdout), `-b/--block-size N`, `@archive` (chain another archive). Extraction: mutex `-k/--keep-old-files`/`--keep-newer-files`, `-m/--modification-time`, `-O/--to-stdout`, `-U/--unlink-first`, `-p/--preserve-permissions`, `--safe-writes` (atomic temp-file extract), `-S` (sparse extraction). Path/link: `-P/--absolute-paths`, `-L/--dereference`, `-H`, `-h`, `-l/--check-links`, `--one-file-system`. Selection: `-C/--cd DIR`, `-T/--files-from FILE`, `-X/--exclude-from FILE`, repeatable `*--exclude PATTERN` + `*--include PATTERN`, `--exclude-vcs`, `-n/--no-recursion`, `--strip-components N`. Ownership: mutex `--same-owner`/`--no-same-owner`, `-o` (overloaded: ustar format in c/r/u, running uid in x), `--uid`/`--gid`/`--uname`/`--gname` overrides, `--numeric-owner`. **`--format` enum** (12 values: `ustar`/`pax`/`v7`/`cpio`/`shar`/`ar`/`mtree`/`iso9660`/`zip`/`7zip`/`xar`/`raw`), `--posix` (= `--format=pax`). Metadata mutex pairs: `--acls` ↔ `--no-acls`, `--xattrs` ↔ `--no-xattrs`, `--fflags` ↔ `--no-fflags` (BSD chflags). Date filtering: 8-flag time-cmp matrix `--newer`/`--newer-mtime`/`--newer-than`/`--newer-mtime-than` and the 4 `--older*` mirrors. Diagnostics: `-v/--verbose`, `-w/--confirmation/--interactive`, `-q/--fast-read`, `--totals`. Misc: `-s+ pattern` (regex name transform), repeatable `*--options opts` (module-specific behavior), `--use-compress-program PROG` (`_command_names -e`), `--null` (NUL-separated file list), `--passphrase PW`, `-B/--read-full-blocks` (GNU compat no-op). Repeatable trailing positional `*:file:_files` for the file/member list. `bsdtar` already in blacklist line 2550; no add needed.
- **Pelletier go-toml v2 family — tomljson + jsontoml + tomll (3 binary stems via single multi-stem file)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-116 `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Single multi-stem file `_tomljson` is `#compdef tomljson jsontoml tomll`, dispatching on `$service` — covers Thomas Pelletier's pair of TOML↔JSON converters plus the in-place TOML linter/formatter from the same module. All three share the upstream `internal/cli/cli.go` argv-handling pattern (bare `flag.Parse()` + positional file or stdin), so the only meaningful CLI flag in the entire family is `jsontoml`'s `-use-json-number`. **`tomljson`** (TOML → JSON): `--help`, repeatable `*:TOML file (stdin if omitted):_files -g "*.(toml|tml)"` (covers both the canonical `.toml` and the historic `.tml` extension occasionally seen in older test corpora). **`jsontoml`** (JSON → TOML): `--help`, `-use-json-number` (preserves int/float precision by unmarshaling numbers as `json.Number` instead of `float64` — relevant for TOML round-trips of integer constants that would otherwise lose precision), repeatable `*:JSON file (stdin if omitted):_files -g "*.json"`. **`tomll`** (TOML lint/reformat): `--help`, repeatable `*:TOML file (lint + reformat in-place):_files -g "*.(toml|tml)"` — operates **in-place** by default per upstream `Inplace: true` in `cmd/tomll/main.go`, so positional completion intentionally doesn't gate on `-i`/`--in-place` flags (they don't exist). - **lziprecover (Antonio Diaz Diaz's data-recovery tool for the lzip format)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname` + the round-116 `#compdef`-line multi-stem grep). Flags transcribed directly from upstream [manpages.debian.org/bookworm/lziprecover/lziprecover.1](https://manpages.debian.org/bookworm/lziprecover/lziprecover.1.en.html). **Candidate-hunt dup-skip log this round (6 already-covered)**: `lzip`/`plzip` already at `more_src/_lzip` + `more_src/_plzip` (and `lzip-decompressor` covered as multi-stem via `src/_lzip-decompressor` `#compdef` line — caught by the round-116 grep upgrade), `pax` caught at stock zsh, `gron`/`huniq`/`fselect`/`sponge` (via multi-stem `more_src/_moreutils`) all already covered. `clzip`/`pdlzip` (C-only / public-domain lzip variants) truly fresh but share `lzip`'s flag set verbatim — could be added as multi-stem to `_lzip` in a future cleanup round; not a separate write. Single-file completion `_lziprecover` covers the data-recovery tool for the lzip format — repairs single-byte errors, splits multi-member archives, dumps/strips/removes corrupt members, and reproduces zeroed sectors using a known-good reference copy. ~26 flags grouped with 2 mutex sets: meta `-h/--help`, `-V/--version`. Core ops (each with `(...)` mutex against `-q` exclusion via `-v` selection): `-a/--trailing-error` (exit non-zero on trailing data), `-A/--alone-to-lz` (lzma-alone format conversion), `-c/--stdout`, `-d/--decompress`, `-D/--range-decompress N-M` (byte-range stdout dump), `-l/--list` (sizes), `-s/--split` (multi-member explode), `-t/--test` (integrity), `-f/--force`, `-k/--keep`. Repair-specific operations: `-e/--reproduce` (zeroed-sector reproduction via reference copy) + 3-flag tuning sub-group `--lzip-level N\|a\|m[N]` (single level / all / match length) / `--lzip-name NAME` (lzip executable, completes via `_command_names -e`) / `--reference-file FILE` (known-good `.lz` via glob); `-R/--repair` (single small-byte error repair); `-m/--merge` (correct errors using multiple corrupted copies of the same file). Output routing: `-o/--output FILE`, `-i/--ignore-errors`. Member-list operations (each takes a `[list]:d:t` spec — list of member ranges, `d` for damaged, `t` for trailing-data): `--dump SPEC` (dump to stdout), `--remove SPEC` (in-place removal), `--strip SPEC` (copy minus listed members). Verbosity mutex `-q/--quiet` ↔ repeatable `*-v/--verbose` (per upstream: `--quiet` cancels out `--verbose` and `-v -v` gives more detail than a single `-v`). Tolerance: `--loose-trailing` (allow trailing data that looks like a corrupt header). Repeatable positional `*:lzip file:_files -g "*.(lz|tlz|lzma)"` covers the 3 lzip-family extensions (.lz canonical / .tlz tar-bundled / .lzma legacy). `lziprecover` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 15184 between `lzip.lzip` and `lzless` (sort verified position-by-position: at index 4 `lzip.lzip`'s '.' (46) < `lziprecover`'s 'r' (114), and at index 2 `lziprecover`'s 'i' (105) < `lzless`'s 'l' (108)). LC_ALL=C sort verified.

Single-file completion `_zoo` covers the classic .zoo archive format (still used for legacy PD shareware archives) — dual-mode CLI: a 17-letter "expert" single-character command verb or a hyphenated 10-verb "novice" form (`-add`/`-extract`/etc) that mirrors the same operations. 17 expert commands enumerated via `_expert` describe: `a` (add — overwrites if newer), `u` (update — newer-only), `c` (comment), `f` (filter — compress/decompress with M/u/h modifiers), `D` (delete inside archive), `e` (extract basename only), `g` (generate sub-archive — `A`/`q`/`+`/`-`/`=` modifiers), `h`/`H` (short/verbose help), `l`/`L` (short/long list), `P` (pack/squeeze), `T` (fix timestamp), `U` (undelete), `v`/`V` (verbose/full-verbose list), `x` (extract preserving paths). 10 novice commands enumerated via `_novice` describe: `-add`/`-freshen`/`-delete`/`-update`/`-extract`/`-move`/`-print`/`-list`/`-test`/`-comment`. Positional 1 uses `_alternative` to multiplex the two command surfaces — users get both expert and novice candidates in a single tab, with type tags distinguishing them. Positional 2 is the archive file (`_files -g "*.(zoo|ZOO)"` for case-insensitive matching since old DOS-era zoo files often used `.ZOO`). Trailing `*:file inside archive:_files` for the file-list arguments. The ~50 sub-command modifiers (e.g. extract modifiers `N`/`O`/`S`/`o`/`p`/`/`/`d`; list modifiers `a`/`A`/`c`/`C`/`d`/`f`/`g`/`m`/`q`/`v`/`V`/`@`/`/`/`1`/`+`/`-`; etc) are documented in the man page but not modeled here — zoo's modifier syntax concatenates them onto the command letter (e.g. `zoo vC archive` for list with column-aligned output) which doesn't tab-complete cleanly; left for manual entry. `zoo` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 29519 between `zoneminder` and `zookeeper-server` (sort verified position-by-position: at index 2 `zoneminder`'s 'n' (110) < `zoo`'s 'o' (111); within the `zoo*` block, `zoo` (length 3) < `zookeeper-server` (length 16) by shorter-string-wins on shared `zoo` prefix). - **vnu (W3C Nu HTML/CSS/SVG validator — Java)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname`). Single-file completion `_vnu` covers the Nu HTML Checker (Java-based — invoked as `java -jar vnu.jar` or the `vnu` wrapper script) — validates URLs/files/directories against W3C schemas for HTML5+/CSS/SVG/XHTML. Sister binaries `vnu-server`/`vnu-client` expose the same checker over HTTP and are out of scope for this completion. ~27 flags grouped with 3 mutex sets: meta `--help`, `--version`. Message filtering: `--asciiquotes` (smart-quote substitution in messages); mutex `--skip-info-messages` ↔ `--errors-only`; `--Werror` (any warning → non-zero exit), `--exit-zero-always` (always 0 even with errors), `--stdout` (errors to stdout not stderr); `--filterfile FILE` (regex pattern file) + repeatable `*--filterpattern REGEX` for selective message suppression. Output format: `--format gnu\|xml\|json\|text` (full upstream enum). **Document-type dispatch mutex** (7-flag exclusion group — only one can be active at a time): `--skip-non-css`/`--css` for CSS-only mode, `--skip-non-svg`/`--svg` for SVG-only mode, `--skip-non-html`/`--html`/`--xml` for parser selection on HTML/XHTML files. Cross-type opt-ins (not in the mutex group since they're additive): `--also-check-css` and `--also-check-svg` for checking CSS+SVG alongside HTML. HTTP fetch: `--user-agent UA-STRING`, repeatable `*--additional-request-header "HEADER: VALUE"` for custom request headers when validating remote URLs. Parser behavior: `--no-langdetect` (skip language detection + `html[lang]` check), `--no-stream` (force buffered instead of streaming parse). Diagnostic: `--verbose` (print file names being checked). Synopsis-only flags reproduced with best-guess arg types: repeatable `*--entities` (extra entity defs) and `--schema URL-OR-FILE` (non-default schema override). Repeatable positional `*:URL/file/directory:_files` covers the three input forms vnu accepts. `vnu` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 27544 between `vnstati` and `void` (sort verified position-by-position: at index 1 both share 'n' (110), so resolves at index 2 — `vnstati`'s 's' (115) < `vnu`'s 'u' (117); and at index 1 `vnu`'s 'n' (110) < `void`'s 'o' (111)).
