- **when (Leon Brocard's tiny personal calendar utility)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname`). Flags + command codes transcribed from upstream [manpages.debian.org/bookworm/when/when.1](https://manpages.debian.org/bookworm/when/when.1.en.html). **Candidate-hunt dup-skip log this round (substantial — 12 caught + 2 deferred)**: 10 already-covered candidates `tdl`/`icdiff`/`pcre2grep`/`deheader`/`cppman`/`calcurse`/`remind`/`pueue`/`autorestic` plus the round-113-promised `strongswan` — `swanctl` man page sourced cleanly but the **stock zsh** at `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh/functions/_swanctl` already ships a `_swanctl` (and similarly `_ipsec`), so neither can be added; the `strongswan` umbrella binary's own man page returned 404 across `manpages.debian.org` dyn-redirect, `man.archlinux.org/man/strongswan.8.en`, and `wiki.strongswan.org/projects/strongswan/wiki/Strongswanctl` (Anubis access-denied) — deferred per the round-106/108/109/111/113 source-404 precedent. `ts` (task spooler) explored as fresh + in blacklist but skipped because the `ts` binary name collides with the unrelated `moreutils ts` timestamp filter — writing a single `_ts` would mismatch one of the two tools depending on which the user installed; deferred for proper multi-tool detection in a future round. Single-file completion `_when` covers the single-file calendar (default `~/.when/calendar`, one line per event) — long-form-only flags drive rendering and an 8-letter positional command code that can be **combined** (e.g. `when cw` = calendars then weekly items, `when iy` = items then year view). 8 command codes via `_verbs` describe: `i` (default — upcoming items), `c` (last/this/next month calendar grids without items), `e` (open `$EDITOR` on the calendar file), `w`/`m`/`y` (coming week/month/year items), `j` (modified Julian day for date arithmetic), `d` (current date only). ~36 long-form flags grouped with 9 mutex pairs encoded in zsh exclusion sets: meta `--help`/`--version`; window control `--language LANG`, `--future DAYS` (default 14), `--past DAYS` (default -1), `--calendar FILE`, `--editor COMMAND` (default `emacs -nw` — completes via `_command_names -e`); wrap mutex `--wrap COLS` / `--wrap_auto` ↔ `--noowrap_auto` / `--wrap_max COLS`; rows mutex `--rows ROWS` (default 40) / `--rows_auto` ↔ `--norows_auto`; header mutex `--header` ↔ `--noheader`; pager mutex `--paging` ↔ `--nopaging` + `--paging_less_options OPTS`; styling `--filter_accents_on_output`, `--styled_output`, `--styled_output_if_not_tty`, `--calendar_today_style STYLE`, `--items_today_style STYLE`; pre-processing `--prefilter PROGRAM` (`_command_names -e`); date control `--now "Y M D"` (override current date); month rendering mutex `--neighboring_months` ↔ `--noneighboring_months`; week-start mutex `--monday_first` ↔ `--nomonday_first`; Easter `--orthodox_easter`; time format mutex `--ampm` ↔ `--noampm` + `--auto_pm HOUR` (assume PM for hours below X); entry expansion mutex `--literal_only` ↔ `--noliteral_only`. `when` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 27913 between `wheel3.9` and `whence` (sort verified position-by-position: at index 3 `wheel3.9`'s 'e' (101) < `when`'s 'n' (110), and at index 4 `when` ends < `whence`'s 'c' (99) — wait, 'c' is 99 not nothing; correct comparison: `when` length-4 vs `whence` length-6, shared prefix `when`, so `when` < `whence` by shorter-string-wins). LC_ALL=C sort verified.

Positional 1 is the output `.djvu` file (via `_files -g "*.djvu"`), repeatable positional 2+ accept chunk specs. The `_describe -S ''` suffix-suppression keeps zsh from auto-inserting a space after the `=` so the user can immediately continue typing the chunk argument. `djvumake` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 6318 between `djvuextract` and `djvups` (sort verified position-by-position: at index 4 `djvuextract`'s 'e' (101) < `djvumake`'s 'm' (109) < `djvups`'s 'p' (112)). Single-file completion `_pngnq` covers the NeuQuant-based PNG palette reducer — maps full-color PNG → 8-bit palette PNG for smaller file size, optional Floyd-Steinberg dithering, default output suffix `-nq8.png`. 10 flags + repeatable positional: meta `-h`, `-V` (version + library versions — the uppercase `-V` distinguishes from the lowercase `-v` verbosity flag, an unusual convention worth honoring); diagnostic `-v` (verbose status messages); safety `-f` (force overwrite existing output); algorithm tuning `-s FACTOR` (NeuQuant sample factor — default 3, higher = faster + less accurate), `-n COLORS` (target palette size — 2..256, default 256), `-Q n\|f` (dither method enum — `n` = no dither/default, `f` = Floyd-Steinberg), `-g GAMMA` (image gamma override — defaults to reading the source PNG's gAMA chunk, falls back 1.0); output routing `-e SUFFIX` (filename suffix override, default `-nq8.png`), `-d DIR` (output directory override — useful for keeping originals untouched); repeatable positional `*:input PNG (stdin if omitted):_files -g "*.png"`. The `-Q n|f` dither enum is encoded as a 2-value choice list so users can't mistype it; sample-factor, color-count, and gamma are left as bare-numeric prompts (no enum) since the upstream-documented "good default" (3) is just a starting hint. `pngnq` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 19993 between `pngfix` and `pngquant` (sort verified position-by-position: at index 3 `pngfix`'s 'f' (102) < `pngnq`'s 'n' (110) < `pngquant`'s 'q' (113)). LC_ALL=C sort verified.

- **Joern family — joern + joern-cli + joern-parse + joern-export + joern-scan + joern-slice + joern-flow + joern-vectors + joern-stats (9 binary stems via single multi-stem file)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` via `-iname`). Single multi-stem file `_joern` is `#compdef joern joern-cli joern-parse joern-export joern-scan joern-slice joern-flow joern-vectors joern-stats`, dispatching on `$service` — covers Whitespace Engineering's static code-analysis platform built around CPGs (Code Property Graphs). **`joern`/`joern-cli`** (interactive Scala REPL launcher): `--help`, `--script FILE` (run script instead of REPL, `.sc`/`.scala` glob), `*--param key=value`, `--import-script FILE`, `--server`/`--server-host HOST`/`--server-port PORT` (JSON-RPC server mode), `--nocolors`. **`joern-parse`** (source → CPG): `-o/--output FILE`, `--language` with 14-frontend enum (`c`/`cpp`/`java`/`jvm`/`javasrc`/`go`/`python`/`php`/`csharp`/`kotlin`/`js`/`javascript`/`ruby`/`swift`/`ghidra`), `--list-languages`, `--namespaces NS,NS`, mutex `--nooverlays` ↔ `--overlaysonly`, `--max-num-def N` (data-flow definition limit), trailing frontend-args after `--`. **`joern-export`** (CPG → graph format): `-o/--out DIR`, `--repr` (7-value: ast/cfg/ddg/cdg/pdg/cpg14/cpg/all, default cpg14), `--format` (4-value: dot/neo4jcsv/graphml/graphson). **`joern-scan`** (run query scans): `--overwrite`, `--store`, `--dump`/`--dump-to FILE`, `--list-query-names`, `--updatedb`/`--dbversion`, `--names NAMES,NAMES` and `--tags TAGS,TAGS` query-set filters, `--depth N` interprocedural call depth, `--language`/`--list-languages` (12-frontend enum). **`joern-slice`** (CPG slicing — state-machine sub-tree with 2 modes): common flags `-o/--out`, `--dummy-types`, `--file-filter`/`--method-name-filter`/`--method-parameter-filter`/`--method-annotation-filter` regex filters, `-p/--parallelism N`; **`data-flow` mode** adds `--slice-depth N` (default 20), `--sink-filter REGEX`, `--end-at-external-method`; **`usages` mode** adds `--min-num-calls N` (default 1), `--exclude-operators`, `--exclude-source`. **`joern-flow`** (data-flow query): 3 positionals `src-regex`/`dst-regex`/`cpg-file`, plus `--src-param N`/`--dst-param N`/`--depth N`/`--verbose`. **`joern-vectors`** (CPG → vectors): `-o/--out DIR`, `--features` flag, positional CPG. **`joern-stats`** (minimal flag set — scopt config not exposed): `--help` + CPG positional. **Blacklist additions (9)**: `joern`, `joern-cli`, `joern-export`, `joern-flow`, `joern-parse`, `joern-scan`, `joern-slice`, `joern-stats`, `joern-vectors` inserted between `joe` and `john` — sort verified position-by-position: at index 2 `joe`'s 'e' (101) = `joern`'s 'e' (101), so `joe` < `joern` by shorter-string-wins (length 3 < 5); within the `joern-*` block, suffix order resolves as `cli` (c=99) < `export` (e=101) < `flow` (f=102) < `parse` (p=112) < `scan` (sc=115,99) < `slice` (sl=115,108) < `stats` (st=115,116) < `vectors` (v=118); finally at index 2 `joern`'s 'e' (101) < `john`'s 'h' (104). - **shellcraft (pwntools' shellcode generator with hierarchical shellcode catalog)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh` — used the upgraded `-iname` (case-insensitive) dup-check this round following last round's macOS HFS+/APFS case-insensitivity gotcha). Single-file completion `_shellcraft` covers Gallopsled's standalone `shellcraft` binary (also reachable as `pwn shellcraft <name>`); generates pre-built shellcodes from a hierarchical catalog (architecture `.` os `.` payload — e.g. `amd64.linux.sh`, `i386.linux.dupsh`, `arm.linux.execve`, `aarch64.linux.sh`, `mips.linux.sh`, `thumb.linux.sh`) with per-name argument lists, plus encoding/output transformations applied after generation. ~20 flags grouped: meta `-h/--help`, `-?/--show` (per-name doc), `-l/--list` (catalog browse, optional filter), `--syscalls` (list all syscalls for selected arch+os, exit); output `-o/--out FILE`, `-f/--format` with the full 18-value upstream enum table (`r`/`raw`, `s`/`str`/`string`, `c`, `h`/`hex`, `a`/`asm`/`assembly`, `p`, `i`/`hexii`, `e`/`elf`, `d`/`escaped`, `default`); debug `-d/--debug` (auto-launch GDB), `-b/--before` and `-a/--after` (insert debug-trap markers around emitted code), `--delim` (multi-shellcode separator); bad-byte encoding `-v/--avoid HEX-BYTES`, `-n/--newline`, `-z/--zero` (NULL-byte avoid — the three classic shellcode-encoding constraints); execution `-r/--run` (run the generated shellcode in-process for quick smoke-test), `--address HEX` (load-address override); ELF emission `-s/--shared` (build shared-library ELF instead of raw blob); pwn-global overrides `--arch` (11-value enum `i386`/`amd64`/`arm`/`aarch64`/`thumb`/`mips`/`mipsel`/`mips64`/`mips64el`/`powerpc`/`sparc`), `--os` (5-value enum `linux`/`freebsd`/`windows`/`baremetal`/`android`); color mutex `--color` ↔ `--no-color`. **`_names` catalog** seeds the positional argument with 21 of the most common CTF picks (amd64+i386+arm+aarch64+mips+thumb x sh/execve/dupsh/read/write/open/connect/listen/cat) plus common synthetic `common.{nop,infloop,debugbreak}` — users still tab through arbitrary names since the upstream catalog is much larger than this seed. Positional argument 2+ is the shellcode-specific argument list (e.g. `i386.linux.read 3 0x8048000 100` for read(fd, buf, len)) — left as free-form `*:shellcode argument:` since arg semantics depend entirely on which shellcode is selected. `shellcraft` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 23534 between `shellcheck` and `shellharden` (sort verified position-by-position: at index 5 both `shellcheck` and `shellcraft` share 'c' (99), so resolves at index 6 — `shellcheck`'s 'h' (104) < `shellcraft`'s 'r' (114); and `shellcraft`'s index-5 'c' (99) < `shellharden`'s index-5 'h' (104)). LC_ALL=C sort verified.
- **one_gadget (David Wang's libc "one gadget RCE" finder)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh`) — flags transcribed directly from upstream [github.com/david942j/one_gadget](https://github.com/david942j/one_gadget) README options table. Single-file completion `_one_gadget` covers the Ruby tool that locates the single-instruction `execve("/bin/sh", NULL, NULL)` shortcut inside a libc image — the bread-and-butter primitive for libc-leak exploits in pwn CTF. **Candidate-hunt dup-skip log**: round 104 fresh-check turned up `ROPgadget` (Jonathan Salwan's ROP gadget finder) which was correctly skipped — existing `more_src/_ROPgadget` (canonical filename `_ropgadget` on disk; macOS HFS+/APFS case-insensitive resolves both spellings) already declares `#compdef ROPgadget ropgadget` with comprehensive flag coverage including `--rawArch`/`--rawMode`/`--rawEndian` capstone enums and `--mipsrop` MIPS-specific dispatch. Note for future fresh-checks: case-insensitive macOS filesystems make `find -name` (case-sensitive) lie about what's already on disk — the file walker resolved the file as `_ropgadget` even though the dup-check name was `_ROPgadget`. 12 flags: meta `-h/--help`, `--version`, `--info BuildID` (show version info for a specific libc BuildID without lookup). Input source: `-b/--build-id BuildID` (SHA1 BuildID lookup against bundled db) versus libc-file positional via `_files -g "*libc*"` — repeatable; mutex `-f/--force-file` ↔ `--no-force-file` controls precedence between file-first vs BuildID-first lookup. Output: `-l/--level 0|1|2|3` (verbosity — higher reveals more conditional/marginal gadgets), `-o/--output-format pretty|raw|json` and `-r/--raw` shorthand (both wired into the same mutex group so zsh suppresses the dominated flag); `-n/--near FUNCTIONS-OR-FILE` orders results by proximity to specified ELF functions or GOT entries (completes via `_files`). Exploit-integration: `-s/--script EXPLOIT-SCRIPT` (execute script per-gadget with the offset as `$1` — heavily used in CTF auto-pwn pipelines); `--base HEX-ADDRESS` (libc base override, default 0). `one_gadget` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 18150 between `ondir` and `oneagent` (sort verified position-by-position: at index 2 `ondir`'s 'd' (100) < `one_gadget`/`oneagent` shared 'e' (101), then at index 3 `one_gadget`'s '_' (95) < `oneagent`'s 'a' (97) — underscore precedes lowercase letters in ASCII so `one_gadget` slots ahead of the `onea*` block). LC_ALL=C sort verified.
- **pwninit (Andrew Otto's CTF binary-exploit challenge initializer)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh`) — flags extracted directly from upstream [github.com/io12/pwninit](https://github.com/io12/pwninit) `src/opts.rs` (structopt definitions that generate clap args). Single-file completion `_pwninit` covers the auto-detection + patchelf + pwntools-template-emission flow used at the start of every pwn CTF challenge. 11 flags: meta `-h/--help`, `-V/--version`. Auto-detect overrides: `--bin FILE` (challenge binary), `--libc FILE` (challenge libc, completes via `_files -g "*libc*"`), `--ld FILE` (linker for libc preload, completes via `_files -g "*ld*"`). Template customization: `--template-path FILE` (custom pwntools solve-script template, completes via `_files -g "*.py"`), `--template-bin-name NAME` (binary-variable name in emitted template, default `exe`), `--template-libc-name NAME` (default `libc`), `--template-ld-name NAME` (default `ld`). Disable switches: `--no-patch-bin` (skip patchelf), `--no-template` (skip solve-script emission). All file-completion specs use targeted globs — `*libc*` matches the typical CTF naming convention (`libc.so.6`, `libc-2.31.so`, `libc6_2.27-3ubuntu1_amd64.deb`-extracted), `*ld*` matches `ld-linux-x86-64.so.2`/`ld-2.31.so`/etc, `*.py` matches the pwntools template. `pwninit` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 20894 between `pwned` and `pwpolicy` (sort verified position-by-position: at index 3 `pwned`'s 'e' (101) < `pwninit`'s 'i' (105), and at index 2 `pwninit`'s 'n' (110) < `pwpolicy`'s 'p' (112) so it remains at the end of the `pwn*` block before `pwp*` begins). - **ptw (pytest-watch — fs-watch-and-rerun harness for pytest)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh`) — flags transcribed directly from upstream [github.com/joeyespo/pytest-watch](https://github.com/joeyespo/pytest-watch) README options table. Single-file completion `_ptw` covers Joe Esposito's pytest-watch — watches the filesystem and re-runs pytest on change. 19 flags total; unknown extra args pass through to pytest. Meta `-h/--help`, `-V/--version`. Watcher filtering: repeatable `*--ignore DIR` (file-set walker excludes), `--ext exts` (comma-separated `.py`/`*.pyx`/etc that trigger re-runs — default `.py`, `*` allows any), `--config FILE` (override implicit config-file lookup). Trigger control: `-c/--clear` (clear screen before each run), `-n/--nobeep`, `-w/--wait` (let a run finish before re-triggering — opposed to default-interrupt-on-fs-event), `--spool ms` (re-run delay default 200ms — lets fs events queue up), `-p/--poll` (polling instead of inotify-style events — useful in VMs/Docker bind mounts). Hook commands (each completes via `_command_names -e`): `--beforerun` (pre-run), `--afterrun` (post-run; gets pytest exit code as `$1`), `--onpass`, `--onfail`, `--onexit`, `--runner` (override the default `pytest` command). Debugger: `--pdb` (start pdb on errors, also implies `--wait` to prevent pdb interruption). Verbosity mutex `-q/--quiet` ↔ `-v/--verbose` (with `--quiet` taking precedence per upstream — encoded as a single mutex group so zsh suppresses the dominated flag once the user has selected). Trailing `*:pytest path or pytest arg:_files` passes through to pytest's own argument parser. `ptw` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 20750 between `ptunnel` and `ptweens` (sort verified position-by-position: at index 2 `ptunnel`'s 'u' (117) < `ptw`'s 'w' (119), and at index 3 `ptw` ends while `ptweens`'s 'e' (101) is present — shorter-string-wins gives `ptw` < `ptweens`). Single-file completion `_ponymix` covers the libpulse-direct mixer (not a pactl wrapper). 12 flags: `-h/--help`, `-V/--version`, `-c/--card CARD` (with `_ponymix_cards` from `ponymix list-cards-short`), `-d/--device DEVICE` (with `_ponymix_devices` device-name + numerical-id alternative — live from `ponymix --<type> list-short`), `-t/--devtype TYPE` (sink/source/sink-input/source-output), 6 shortcut aliases `--source`/`--input` (devtype=source), `--sink`/`--output` (devtype=sink), `--sink-input`, `--source-output` — encoded as mutex set against `-t/--devtype`, `-N/--notify` (desktop-notify on action). 24 verbs from upstream `verbs=` array via `_verbs` describe: `help`, `defaults`, `set-default`, `list`, `list-short`, `list-cards`, `list-cards-short`, `get-volume`, `set-volume`, `get-balance`, `set-balance`, `adj-balance`, `increase`, `decrease`, `mute`, `unmute`, `toggle`, `is-muted`, `move`, `kill`, `list-profiles`, `list-profiles-short`, `get-profile`, `set-profile`. Pre-scan loop over `$words` detects devtype hint from any `--sink`/`--source`/`-t`/`--devtype=`/`--sink-input`/`--source-output` already on the command line so live device discovery matches user intent. Per-verb argument completion: `set-volume`/`increase`/`decrease` accept `+N`/`-N`/`N` percent (free-form `_message`); `set-balance`/`adj-balance` take signed value (-100..100); `set-default`/`kill` complete via `_ponymix_devices`; `move` takes two positionals (source then target, both via `_ponymix_devices`); `set-profile` completes via `_ponymix_profiles` (live `ponymix list-profiles-short`); other verbs (`mute`/`unmute`/`toggle`/`is-muted`/`get-volume`/`get-balance`/`get-profile`/list/defaults/help) emit "no further arguments". `ponymix` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 20148 between `ponyc` and `ponysay` (lexicographic-by-position-4: 'c' < 'm' < 's'). LC_ALL=C sort verified.
- **resperf (DNS resolver perf testing tool — DNS-OARC dnsperf package)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh`) — flags transcribed directly from upstream [manpages.debian.org/bookworm/dnsperf/resperf.1](https://manpages.debian.org/bookworm/dnsperf/resperf.1.en.html). Single-file completion `_resperf` covers DNS-OARC's resolver-side load tester (sister to the authoritative-server-side `dnsperf` already in repo at `more_src/_dnsperf`). resperf ramps up query rate over a configurable ramp-up window, optionally sustains constant load after, and finds the throughput threshold under a target acceptable loss percentage. 27 flags covered: sources `-d FILE` (query input, `_files`; stdin if omitted), `-R` (reopen datafile if exhausted); target `-s HOST` (server, default 127.0.0.1, via `_hosts`), `-p PORT`, `-M MODE` (`udp`/`tcp`/`dot`/`doh`), `-f FAMILY` (`inet`/`inet6`/`any`); rate model `-m QPS` (target max, default 100000), `-r SECONDS` (ramp-up, default 60), `-c SECONDS` (constant-rate hold after ramp, default 0), `-L PERCENT` (max acceptable loss for throughput determination), `-q N` (max outstanding per client, default 64k), `-F N` (fall-behind limit, default 1000; 0=disable); client model `-C N` (clients with separate sockets), `-a ADDR` (local source addr via `_hosts`), `-x PORT` (local source port, default wildcard 0); EDNS/DNSSEC `-D` (DNSSEC OK bit, enables EDNS0), `-e` (EDNS0 OPT only); auth `-y [alg:]name:base64-secret` (TSIG); buffers `-b kB` (socket buffer); plotting `-i SECONDS` (data-point interval, default 0.5), `-P FILE` (output, default `resperf.gnuplot`); protocol-specific `*-O option=value` (repeatable, for DoT/DoH params); timeout `-t SECONDS` (default 45); output `-v` (verbose), `-W` (warnings to stdout); help `-h`. `resperf` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 22089 between `respberry` and `responder` (lexicographic-by-position-4: 'b' < 'e' < 'o'). LC_ALL=C sort verified.
- **powerstat (Canonical's power + thermal + CPU C-state monitor)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh`) — flags transcribed directly from upstream [manpages.ubuntu.com/manpages/jammy/man8/powerstat.8](https://manpages.ubuntu.com/manpages/jammy/man8/powerstat.8.html). Single-file completion `_powerstat` for Colin King's power-monitoring tool that reads either battery discharge rate or RAPL (Running Average Power Limit) domain counters. 19 flags covered: roll-up `-a` (= `-c -f -t -H`); sampling controls `-b` (redo if <98% CPU idle), `-d SECONDS` (start delay — defaults 180s on battery / 0s on RAPL), `-i PERCENT` (idle threshold for forced re-sample), `-p` (redo on any fork/exec/exit), `-r` (redo only if not-idle + fork/exec/exit), `-S` (standard averaging instead of rolling); data collection `-c` (per-CPU C-state activity), `-D` (all power-domain readings), `-f` (avg frequency across on-line cores), `-g` (Intel i915 GPU power), `-H` (histogram of power measurements), `-R` (switch from battery to RAPL source), `-t` (thermal-zone temperatures), `-z` (ignore zero readings); output `-n` (no column headings); log `-s` (dump fork/exec/exit log at end); `-h` (help). Positional args: `1: delay seconds`, `2: number of samples`. `powerstat` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 20239 between `powershell-empire` and `powertop` (lexicographic-by-position-6: 'h' < 's' < 't'). LC_ALL=C sort verified.
- **pacapt (universal pacman-style package-manager wrapper)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh`) — operation/flag inventory extracted directly from upstream [github.com/icy/pacapt](https://github.com/icy/pacapt) README. Single-file completion `_pacapt` for the pacman-API wrapper that translates `-S/-R/-Q/-U` operations into the host system's native package manager (apt/dnf/yum/zypper/brew/portage/pkg/etc). Top-level operation enumeration uses `_alternative` to multiplex two surfaces: **33-op pacman-style fused flag tree** via `_ops` describe (`-S` install, `-Sy` refresh DB, `-Su` upgrade, `-Suy`/`-Syu` refresh+upgrade, `-Ss` search, `-Si`/`-Sii` info/detailed-info, `-Sg` groups, `-Sl` list-repo, `-Sc`/`-Scc`/`-Sccc` cache cleanup graduations, `-Sw` download-only, `-R` remove, `-Rs` remove+deps, `-Rn` remove+configs, `-Rns` remove+deps+configs, `-Rdd` force-skip-dep-check, `-Q` query, `-Qs` query-by-pattern, `-Qi`/`-Qii` info, `-Ql` list-files, `-Qo` owner-of-file, `-Qm` foreign packages, `-Qu` upgradeable, `-Qd` dependencies, `-Qe` explicit-installs, `-Qc` changelog, `-Qk` integrity-verify, `-U` local-file install, `-P` list-supported-ops); **7-alias long-form tree** via `_aliases` describe (`install`/`remove`/`search`/`upgrade`/`update`/`autoremove`/`clean`). Shared `_global` array (6 modifier flags) re-applied per-op: `-h/--help`, `-V/--version`, `--noconfirm`, `-q/--quiet`, `-y` (auto-yes alias), `-w` (download-only alias). Per-op argument handling: install/upgrade/sw/info/list ops accept package args via `_pacapt_remote` helper (deferred — no remote lookup, pacapt already translates underneath); search/`-Ss`/`-Qs` accept free-form pattern; remove/`-Q*` query ops complete from live `pacapt -Qq` via `_pacapt_installed` helper; `-Qo` completes file paths via `_files`; `-U` completes local package files via `_files -g "*.(deb|rpm|pkg.tar.{zst,xz,gz}|apk|tgz)"` glob covering Debian/RPM/Arch-zst/Arch-xz/Arch-gz/Alpine/tarball; cache cleanup ops (`-Sc`/`-Scc`/`-Sccc`/`autoremove`/`clean`) and `update`/`-P` take no positional args. `pacapt` added to `blacklist.txt` at line 18571 between `pac` and `pacaptr` (Rust rewrite — distinct binary already covered). LC_ALL=C sort verified.
- **gm (GraphicsMagick — single-binary image-processing suite)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh`) — subcommand inventory + flag coverage extracted from [manpages.debian.org/bookworm/graphicsmagick/gm.1](https://manpages.debian.org/bookworm/graphicsmagick/gm.1.en.html) and the upstream [graphicsmagick.org reference](http://www.graphicsmagick.org/GraphicsMagick.html). Single-file completion `_gm` dispatches the 14-subcommand utility tree: `animate` (X11 animation viewer), `batch` (linear gm-script executor), `benchmark` (perf-iteration meta), `compare` (diff statistics across metrics), `composite` (blend/merge), `conjure` (MSL — Magick Scripting Language interpreter), `convert` (format conversion + transform pipeline), `display` (X11 viewer), `help` (per-subcommand help), `identify` (image format/characteristics report), `import` (X11 window capture), `mogrify` (in-place transform — overwrites originals), `montage` (tiled composite), `time` (CPU+wall-time meta), `version` (release + features report). Per-utility specialization: `identify` (own subset — `-format` escape-string, `-ping`, `-regard-warnings`, `-size`, `-depth`, `-debug`); `display`/`animate` (X11 + animation timing: `*-delay`, `*-pause`, `*-loop`, `*-magnify`, `*-immutable`, `*-treedepth`); `import` (X11 capture: `*-crop`, `-frame`, `-border`, `-delay`, `-mosaic`, `-screen`, `-silent`, `-snaps`); `benchmark` (`-duration`, `-iterations`, `-stepthreads`, `-rawcsv`, recursive subcommand dispatch via `->sub` state); `time` (recursive subcommand dispatch); `conjure` (MSL: repeatable `*-set name=value`, `-monitor`, `-verbose`, `-debug`, `*.msl` file glob); `batch` (`-echo`, `-feedback`, `-pass`, `-fail`, `-prompt`, `-escape` none/windows, `-stop-on-error`). Image input completion uses `_files -g "*.(#i)(jpg|jpeg|png|gif|bmp|tif|tiff|webp|heic|heif|avif|svg|pdf|psd|tga|xpm|xbm|pnm|ppm|pgm|pbm|png|ico|jp2|jxr|jxl|dds|dpx|exr|hdr|miff|mng|sgi|yuv|xcf|wmf|mvg)"` for case-insensitive multi-format matching. `gm` already at blacklist line 9519 (between `glx-utils` and `gm2`); no add needed.

Single-file completion `_git-revise` for Michael Sullivan's efficient non-interactive history editor (update/split/rearrange commits without rebase mechanics). - **rdisc6 (IPv6 Router Discovery) + tracepath (MTU-aware tracer) + iptables save/restore** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh`) — all from man.archlinux.org / manpages.debian.org. `rdisc6` (ICMPv6 Router Discovery — send Router Solicitation + print Router Advertisements. 10 flags: `-h/--help`, `-V/--version`, 2-way mutex `-1/--single` (exit on first) / `-m/--multiple` (wait + print all — default), `-n/--numeric` no DNS resolution, 2-way mutex `-q/--quiet` (only prefixes) / `-v/--verbose` (default), `-r/--retry N` retries (default 3), `-s/--source IP` source address, `-w/--wait MS` per-retry wait (default 4000); positional network interface), `tracepath` + `tracepath6` (multi-stem `#compdef tracepath tracepath6` — trace path discovering MTU along the way; no admin privileges required. 8 flags: `-V`, 2-way mutex `-4`/`-6`, 2-way mutex `-n` numeric / `-b` both, `-l BYTES` initial packet size (default 65535 IPv4 / 128000 IPv6), `-m HOPS` max TTL (default 30), `-p PORT` start probe port; positional `<host> [port]`), `iptables-save` + `ip6tables-save` (multi-stem `#compdef iptables-save ip6tables-save` — dump current rules. 4 flags: `-M PATH`/`--modprobe`, `-f FILE`/`--file` (default stdout), `-c/--counters` include packet/byte counters, `-t TABLE`/`--table` filter/nat/mangle/raw/security), `iptables-restore` + `ip6tables-restore` (multi-stem — restore rules from file. 9 flags: `-h/--help`, `-V/--version`, `-c/--counters`, `-n/--noflush` preserve existing, `-t/--test` parse+construct no-commit, stackable `*-v/--verbose`, `-w/--wait [SEC]` xtables-lock wait, `-M/--modprobe`, `-T/--table NAME` restore only this table; positional file). - **lsmod (Linux kmod module list) + niv (Nix dependency manager)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh`) — `lsmod` (Linux kmod from man/lsmod.8 — list currently loaded Linux kernel modules. 4 flags only: `-h/--help`, `-V/--version`, `-s/--syslog` (send errors to syslog instead of stderr), `-v/--verbose` (print what the program is doing — normally silent unless something goes wrong)), `niv` (nmattia/niv from README + src/Niv/Cli.hs — Haskell-based Nix dependency manager; maintains `nix/sources.json` + `nix/sources.nix`. 6 subcommands: `init` (bootstrap with `--latest` for niv branch override), `add` (with `-n/--name`, `-b/--branch`, `-v/--version`, `-t/--template URL`, `-T/--type file|tarball`, repeatable `-a/--attribute k=v`, positional `owner/repo` or URL — supports private GitHub via SSH/`.netrc`), `update` (same flags as add; omit package name to update all; supports `NIV_OVERRIDE_<name>` env vars for local dev), `drop` (positional package), `modify` (change attributes without fetching), `show` (positional package, omit = show all). Shared root flags: `-s/--sources-file` alternate sources.json path, `--no-colors`, `-h/--help`).
- **Sysinternals ProcMon for Linux + rsign/rsign2 Rust Minisign** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh`) — `procmon` (Microsoft Sysinternals/ProcMon-for-Linux from src/configuration/procmon_configuration.cpp — Linux port of the famous Windows Sysinternals Process Monitor. Requires sudo. 7 flags: `-p/--pids CSV` PIDs (capped at MAX_PIDS), `-s/--storageEngine` backend (validated against supported options), `-e/--events CSV` syscalls (default: trace all), `-c/--collect [FILE]` headless mode w/ optional output file (default pattern `procmon_[date]_[time].db`), `-f/--file` load existing trace, `-l/--log` debug trace file path, `-h/--help`. Note: the `-c` and `-f` flags are incompatible with curses UI), `rsign` + `rsign2` (jedisct1/rsign2 — Rust implementation of Minisign for signing files + verifying signatures. Pure Rust, minimal deps. Multi-stem `#compdef rsign rsign2` since binary ships as both names. 3 subcommands: `generate` (-p public-key path default `rsign.pub`, -s secret-key path default `~/.rsign/rsign.key`, mutex -W/--unencrypted password-less + no-encrypt, -f overwrite existing), `sign` (-s secret-key, -x signature output default `<input>.minisig`, -t trusted comment SIGNED, -c untrusted comment, -W password-less, file positional), `verify` (mutex -p public-key-file vs -P public-key-string-arg, -x signature file, -q quiet, -o output content on success, file positional). Global `-h/--help`/`-V/--version`).
- **donut (PIC shellcode generator) + microsocks (tiny SOCKS5 proxy)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh`) — `donut` (TheWover/donut from donut.c usage block — generate position-independent shellcode from .NET assemblies, EXEs, DLLs, and scripts; authorized security-testing tool present in many pentest distributions. 21 flags grouped: module options (`-n/--modname`, `-s/--server host[user:pass]`, `-e/--entropy 1=none|2=random-names|3=random-names+encryption`), PIC options (`-a/--arch 1=x86|2=amd64|3=both`, `-o/--output` default `loader.bin`, `-f/--format 1=bin|2=base64|3=c|4=ruby|5=python|6=powershell|7=csharp|8=hex`, `-y/--fork OFFSET` thread-at-offset, `-x/--exit 1=thread|2=process|3=block`), file options (`-c/--class` REQUIRED for .NET DLL, `-d/--domain` AppDomain, `-i/--input` file, `-m/--method` REQUIRED for .NET DLL, `-p/--params` args, `-w/--unicode` Unicode for unmanaged DLL, `-r/--runtime` CLR version, `-t/--thread` EXE entrypoint as thread), additional (`-z/--compress 1=none|2=aPLib|3=LZNT1|4=Xpress`, `-b/--bypass 1=none|2=abort|3=continue` AMSI/WLDP/ETW, `-k/--headers 1=overwrite|2=keep` PE headers, `-j/--decoy` optional decoy module)), `microsocks` (rofl0r/microsocks from sockssrv.c getopt — tiny SOCKS5 proxy server (<1000 SLOC, single binary). 8 short flags only: `-1` auth_once mode (auth'd IPs added to whitelist for passwordless reconnects), `-q` quiet, `-i` listening IP (default `0.0.0.0`), `-p` listening port (default 1080), `-u`/`-P` user/pass (must be used together), `-b` bind outgoing connections to specific IP, `-w` CSV whitelist of IPs that bypass auth).
- **nfdump tool family deep-dive: 4 NEW + 3 in-place REWRITES in src/** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh`) — all from phaag/nfdump man/*.1 manpages. NEW: `nfpcapd` (pcap-to-nfdump converter; live-capture or read-file mode. 25 flags: input (`-i` iface, `-r` pcap input, `-s` snaplen, `-B` cache size, `-e active,inactive` flow expiry), output (`-w` flow dir, `-p` pcap dir, `-H host[/port]` forward, `-S 0-15` subdir layout, `-t` rotation sec, `-z lzo|bz2|lz4|zstd` with optional levels), daemon (`-D`, `-d`, `-v`, `-u`/`-g` drop-privs, `-P` pidfile), processing (`-I` ident, repeatable `*-o` option CSV, `-W` workers)), `ft2nfdump` (flow-tools-to-nfdump converter — 7 flags: `-r` ft input, `-w` nf output, `-z` compress, `-E` show flows on screen, `-c N` stop after N records, `-h`/`-V`), `geolookup` (GeoIP/ASN lookup helper — 3 flags: `-d DIR` CSV input dir to build DB, `-w` output DB file, `-G` use existing binary DB for queries; positional IP/AS queries), `torlookup` (Tor exit-node lookup helper — 3 flags: `-d DIR` CSV input dir, `-w` output torDB, `-H` use existing torDB; positional IP queries). REWRITES in-place in src/ (moved updated content from more_src/ → src/ to avoid shadow duplication): `nfanon` (was missing `-K` encryption key + `-v`/`-W` flags; had `-M`/`-R` that don't exist upstream — fixed to 6 real flags: `-h`/`-r`/`-w`/`-K`/`-v`/`-W`), `nfexpire` (was missing `-T` runtime/`-p` print profiles/`-Y` confirm-all — added 11 real flags incl. `-l`/`-r`/`-e` dir-modes, `-s`/`-t`/`-w` size/age/watermark thresholds, `-u` collector log path), `nfreplay` (existing had typo `-H /ip>`, missing `-S` source spoof/`-u` usec delay/`-B` buffer/`-z` time-scaling/`-v 5|9|ipfix` version; fixed to 14 real flags). NOTE: existing `_nfprofile` left untouched; existing `_nfcapd` in src/ also untouched (covers main nfdump capture daemon — different from nfpcapd which is pcap-based).
- **Network-flow accounting daemons + LTTng crash recovery** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh`) — `sfcapd` (phaag/nfdump from man/sfcapd.1 — sFlow v4/v6 collector daemon paired with nfdump. 28 short flags: storage (`-w` flow dir, `-C` extra-config, `-z lzo|bz2|lz4|zstd` compress, `-S 0-15` subdir layout, `-t` rotation sec), daemon (`-D` daemonize, `-u`/`-g` drop-privs, `-P` pidfile), network (`-p` UDP port default 9995, `-d` ERSPAN iface, `-I` ident, `-b` bind, mutex `-4`/`-6`, `-j` multicast group, `-R` packet repeater target + `-A` spoof mode, `-B` buffer size), exporters (repeatable `*-n` netflow-source spec, `-M` dynamic exporter dir, `-i`/`-m` flow-metric exporter), processing (`-o gre` options, `-e` auto-expire, `-x` rotation cmd, repeatable `*-X` extensions, `-W` worker threads, `-v 0-4` verbosity)), `sfacctd` (pmacct/pmacct from src/sfacctd.c — pmacct sFlow accounting daemon collecting v2/v4/v5 samples and routing to plugins. 30 short flags: network (`-L` bind IP, `-l` UDP port), aggregation (`-a` list primitives, `-c` aggregation method, `-n` networks/ASNs file, `-t` ports file, repeatable `*-P memory|print|mysql|pgsql|sqlite3|amqp|kafka|tee` plugins), daemon (`-D`, `-d` debug, `-S auth|mail|daemon|kern|user|local0-7` syslog, `-F` pidfile), processing (`-R` renormalize, `-u` numeric protos, `-I` pcap savefile + `-Z`/`-W`/`-Y` replay control, `-T config|setup` dry-run, memory plugin tuning `-p`/`-b`/`-m`/`-s`, `-r` refresh, `-O formatted|csv|json|avro`/`-o`/`-M`/`-A`/`-E` output)), `uacctd` (pmacct/pmacct from src/uacctd.c — pmacct user-space accounting daemon for Netlink NFLOG packets. 26 short flags: same shape as sfacctd MINUS sFlow-network flags, PLUS Netlink-specific (`-g` NFLOG group, `-L` snapshot length); plugin list adds `nfprobe`/`sfprobe`), `lttng-crash` (lttng.org/man/1/lttng-crash/v2.13/ — LTTng v2.13 tool to recover + view traces from shared memory after a crashed system. 6 flags: `-h/--help`, `-V/--version`, `--list-options`, `-x/--extract DIR` extract-only (skip reader), stackable `*-v/--verbose` (up to 3), `-e/--viewer babeltrace|babeltrace2`. Required positional `SHMDIR` (shared-memory dir from `--shm-path`)).
- **LTTng tracing daemons: lttng-sessiond + lttng-relayd** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh`) — `lttng-sessiond` (LTTng v2.13 session daemon — manages tracing sessions, coordinates kernel + 32/64-bit userspace consumers — from lttng.org/man/8/lttng-sessiond/v2.13/. 30+ flags across categories: daemon lifecycle (mutex `-b/--background` keep-FDs vs `-d/--daemonize` close-FDs, `-f/--config *.ini`, `-g/--group` Unix tracing-group default `tracing`, `-l/--load` session config path, `-S/--sig-parent` USR1-on-ready), kernel tracing (`--no-kernel`, `--kmod-probes CSV`, `--extra-kmod-probes CSV`), socket paths (`--agent-tcp-port`, `-a/--apps-sock`, `-c/--client-sock`, full `--consumerd32-{path,libdir}` + `--consumerd64-{path,libdir}` + `--kconsumerd-{cmd,err}-sock` + `--ustconsumerd{32,64}-{cmd,err}-sock` matrix), event notifier (`--event-notifier-error-buffer-size-{kernel,userspace}` slots), verbosity (mutex `-q/--quiet` vs stackable `*-v/--verbose` up to `-vvv`, `--verbose-consumer`), program info (`-h/--help`, `-V/--version`, `--list-options`)), `lttng-relayd` (LTTng relay daemon — receives trace data over network + writes to local storage. 14 flags: lifecycle (mutex `-b/--background` vs `-d/--daemonize`, `-f/--config *.ini`, `-x/--disallow-clear`, `--fd-pool-size`, `-g/--group`, `-w/--working-directory`, stackable `*-v/--verbose`), output grouping (mutex `-p/--group-output-by-host` vs `-s/--group-output-by-session`, `-o/--output DIR`), network ports (`-C/--control-port` default `tcp://0.0.0.0:5342` / `-D/--data-port` default `tcp://0.0.0.0:5343` / `-L/--live-port` default `tcp://localhost:5344`), program info (`-h/--help`, `-V/--version`, `--list-options`)). NOTE: existing `_lttng` covers the lttng(1) client tool itself; this round adds the two daemons.
- **bpftune (Oracle eBPF kernel autotuner) + packetdrill (Google TCP/UDP stack test framework) + rabins (argus binner)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh`) — `bpftune` (oracle/bpftune from src/bpftune.c getopt_long — eBPF-based kernel sysctl auto-tuner. 14 flags: `-h/--help`, `-V/--version`, repeatable `*-a/--allow TUNER` allowlist, `-c/--cgroup DIR`, `-d/--debug`, `-D/--daemon` daemonize, `-l/--libdir DIR`, `-L/--legacy` force-legacy-BPF, `-r/--learning_rate RATE`, `-p/--port PORT`, `-q/--query QUERY` client-query-mode, `-R/--rollback`, `-s/--stderr` log-to-stderr, `-S/--support` print BPF support level), `packetdrill` (google/packetdrill from gtests/net/packetdrill/config.c long_options[] — DSL scripts test TCP/UDP/IP stack behavior with millisecond-precision timing. 3 modes: local (default), wire client (`--wire_server_at HOST:PORT`), wire server (`--wire_server`). 38 flags incl. `--ip_version ipv4|ipv4-mapped-ipv6|ipv6`, `--bind_port`/`--connect_port`, IP config (`--remote_ip`/`--local_ip`/`--gateway_ip`/`--netmask_ip`), link tuning (`--speed Mbps`/`--mss`/`--mtu`), code blocks (`--code_command`/`--code_format python`/`--code_sockopt`), init scripts (`--init_scripts CSV`), timing tolerance (`--tolerance_usecs`/`--tolerance_percent`), wire mode (3-way mutex `--wire_client`/`--wire_server`/`--wire_server_at` + `--wire_server_{ip,port,dev}`/`--wire_client_dev`), shared-object init (`--so_filename *.so`/`--so_flags`), TCP timestamp (`--tcp_ts_ecr_scaled`/`--tcp_ts_tick_usecs`), `--strict_segments`, `--non_fatal TYPES`, `--dry_run`, `--is_anyip`, `--send_omit_free`, `--psp_udp_port`, `--debug`, repeatable `*-D/--define symbol=value`, `-v/--verbose`; positional `*.pkt` scripts), `rabins` + `rabins2` (argus-client(1) Debian manpage — process argus records into time/count/size BINS. Multi-stem `#compdef rabins rabins2`. Subset of `_ra_common` (key ra(1) flags) plus rabins-specific: `-B SECS` bin holding-time, `-M time|count|size|hard|nomodify` combinable strategy modes, repeatable `*-m AGG_OBJ` aggregation object (28 choices same as ratop: srcid/smac/dmac/...sas/das/ias), `-P FIELD` output sort field (distinct from `-m`), `-w FILE` output filename supporting `$field` substitution + strftime). Note `_ra` separately covers ra/ratop/ralabel/rasort/racount/rasplit.
- **Argus network-flow client family (ra/ratop/ralabel/rasort/racount/rasplit)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh`) — `_ra` multi-stem `#compdef ra ratop ralabel rasort racount rasplit` covers the QoSient argus-clients suite for network flow record analysis. Single file with shared `_ra_common` array containing the 28 base ra(1) options (`-A` agg-stats, `-b` dump-compiled-match-code, `-c CHAR` delim, `-D 1-8` debug level, `-d` daemon toggle, `-e REGEX` user-data match, `-E FILE` rejected-records output, `-F CONF` config source, `-h` help, `-H` abbreviate numerics, `-L N` header label frequency, `-n` number-to-name toggle, `-N N` first-N-records, `-p DIGITS` float precision, `-q` quiet, `*-r FILE` read argus data (repeatable, `*.argus`/`*.arg`), `-R DIR` recurse dir, `*-s FIELD` print-fields (repeatable: stime/saddr/daddr/sport/dport/proto/bytes/...), `-S URI` remote source `[user[:pass]@]host[:port]`, `-t TIMERANGE` time filter, `-T SECS` remote-read duration, `-u` Unix-time format, `-w FILE` append output (argus format), `-X` reset to defaults, `-z` TCP-state status field, `-Z s|d|b` actual TCP flag values). Then `case $service` dispatches tool-specific flags: `ratop` adds `-m` aggregation object (28 choices: srcid/smac/dmac/saddr/daddr/matrix/proto/sport/dport/...) + `-M correct|nocorrect|preserve|nopreserve|norep|rmon|nocurses` curses mode; `ralabel` adds `-f LABEL_SPEC_FILE` + `-M ADDR` simple-list mode + `-m saddr|daddr|saddr,daddr` IANA label target; `rasort` adds repeatable `*-m FIELD` sort key (35 choices: stime/ltime/dur/bytes/pkts/saddr/daddr/sport/dport/scc/dcc/sas/das/...) + `-M replace` in-place overwrite; `racount` adds `-M proto|addr` count breakdown (IPv4/IPv6 unicast/multicast addr type, IP/ether/ARP/RARP protos); `rasplit` adds `-M MODE` for partitioning. All variants accept BPF-style filter expression as `*` positional. Verified via argus-client(1) Debian manpages (ratop.1/ralabel.1/rasort.1/racount.1/ra.1). NOTE: existing `_argus` covers the argus(8) collector daemon itself separately.
- **bgpdump (RIPE NCC MRT parser) + irrd (Internet Routing Registry Daemon)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh`) — `bgpdump` (RIPE-NCC/bgpdump from bgpdump.c usage block — MRT-format BGP routing-dump parser maintained by RIPE NCC since 2005, originally Dan Ardelean. 12 short flags only (no long forms): 3-way mutex output modes `-H` multi-line human (default) / `-m` one-line Unix timestamps / `-M` one-line human timestamps; `-O FILE` redirect output; 2-way mutex log destination `-s` syslog (default) / `-v` stderr; `-q` quiet; `-t dump|change` timestamp source for `-m`/`-M`; `-p` packet index at second position; `-l` large communities after regular; `-u` unassigned attributes in one-line mode; `-T` run unit tests + exit. Legacy flags `-i`/`-f`/`-o` recognized but ignored upstream — omitted from completion. MRT file positionals match `*.mrt`/`*.bz2`/`*.gz`/`*.bgp`), `irrd` (irrdnet/irrd from irrd/daemon/main.py argparse — Internet Routing Registry Daemon serving RPSL objects + RPKI integration. Daemon CLI is intentionally minimal — only 2 flags: `--config FILE` alternative YAML config path, `--foreground` do-not-detach. All operational config is YAML-driven). NOTE: existing `_bird` already covers `bird/bird2/birdc/bird6` multi-stem (BIRD routing daemon with all 12 verified flags from sysdep/unix/main.c getopt `"bc:dD:ps:P:u:g:flRh"` — no rewrite needed).
- **brimcap (Brim pcap analyzer) + cshark (CloudShark capture client)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh`) — `brimcap` (brimdata/brimcap from cmd/brimcap/*/command.go — search/analyze/inspect pcap files, drives Zeek + Suricata analyzers to emit ZNG/ZSON/NDJSON; NOT cobra — uses Brim's charm-spec CLI framework with single-dash long opts. 8 subcommands: `analyze` (-nostats, -z ZSON output, pcap positional), `config` (print config), `cut` (-r input, -w output), `index` (-r/-x/-n 10000 default size limit, -root common index dir for parallel search), `info` (no flags; pcap positional), `search` (-w + 7 search flags incl. REQUIRED `-ts` timestamp / `-proto tcp|udp|icmp` / `-src.ip` / `-dst.ip` + optional `-src.port` / `-dst.port` / `-duration 1ns` default), `slice` (-r/-w/-x index file/-from time/-to time/-p proto), `ts` (-r/-w timestamps). Root-only shared flags `-config` (env BRIMCAP_CONFIG) and `-root` (env BRIMCAP_ROOT) injected via SetRootOnlyFlags into analyze/config/search. Root persistent: `-json` (auto-true when stderr not a TTY)), `cshark` (cloudshark/cshark from src/cshark.c getopt `"i:w:s:T:P:S:p:kvh"` — OpenWrt-focused traffic capture + upload to cloudshark.org. 10 short flags only (no long forms): `-h` help, `-v` version, `-i IFACE` listen interface, `-w FILE` write raw packets, `-s BYTES` snarf snaplen, `-k` keep file after upload, `-T SEC` timeout (0=no), `-P N` packet limit (0=no), `-S BYTES` byte limit (0=no), `-p FILE` save PID).
- **ply (lightweight Linux BPF tracer, dtrace/awk-style) + tcpsnitch (LD_PRELOAD sockets API tracer)** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh`) — `ply` (wkz/ply from src/ply/ply.c getopt_long — Tobias Waldekranz's lightweight dynamic Linux tracer. Compiles dtrace/awk-style scripts to BPF via kprobes/tracepoints; only libc required at runtime. Multi-arch (x86_64/aarch64/arm/loongarch/mips/riscv32/riscv64/powerpc). 9 flags: `-h/--help`, `-v/--version`, `-c/--command CMD` (run shell command + exit when done), `-d/--debug`, `-e/--dry-run` (compile-only — no BPF load), `-k/--keep-going` (tolerate trace-buffer overruns), `-S/--dump` (show generated BPF), `-T/--self-test`, `-u/--unbuffer` (force stdout/stderr unbuffered); positional ply script e.g. `'kretprobe:vfs_read { @["size"] = quantize(retval); }'`), `tcpsnitch` (GregoryVds/tcpsnitch from bin/tcpsnitch bash getopts — LD_PRELOAD-based sockets API tracer that intercepts libc network calls. Records tcp_info socket option at user-defined intervals + .pcap per socket. Two modes: Linux (run app directly) or Android (API 23+ via `-a` launch + `-k` kill+pull). 14 flags: `-h` help, `--version`, `-a` Android launch, `-k PKG` Android kill+pull, `-b BYTES` tcp_info dump every N bytes (default 0=off), `-c` pcap capture (Linux only), `-d DIR` trace output dir (default random `/tmp` dir), `-f LEVEL` file log verbosity 0-5 (default 2), `-l LEVEL` stderr log verbosity 0-5 (default 2), `-n` no upload to tcpsnitch.org, `-p` pedantic confirmation mode, `-t MSEC` JSON dump interval (default 1000ms), `-u USEC` tcp_info dump every N µs (default 0=off), `-v` verbose; positional `<app> [<args>]` is the command/package to instrument). Disk-pressure note: `_tcpsnitch` was written via Bash heredoc as a workaround after the Write tool hit ENOSPC at 99.9% disk usage — the underlying volume had only 945Mi free of 926Gi.
- **traceectl (tracee control CLI) + pyrra (SLO management) — both NEW with deep subcommand maps** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh`) — `traceectl` (aquasecurity/tracee from cmd/traceectl/cmd/{root,event,stream,metrics,version}.go cobra — control CLI for a running tracee server. 4 top-level subcommands: `event` (with nested `enable EVENT`/`disable EVENT`/`describe [EVENT]`), `stream` (real-time gRPC consumer with `*POLICIES` filter), `metrics` (tracee performance + resource stats), `version`. Shared flags `--server` (unix socket path, default `client.DefaultSocket`), `--format table/json`, `--output` (dest, default stdout). The `event describe` form lists all events when called with no arg, describes a single event when given one), `pyrra` (pyrra-dev/pyrra from main.go kong — SLO management CLI: define Service Level Objectives in YAML, generates Prometheus rules + UI. 4 top-level subcommands: `api`/`filesystem`/`kubernetes`/`generate` with shared `_shared_prometheus` (`--prometheus-url` default `http://localhost:9090`, `--external-url` for alert annotations, `--enable-prometheus3-migration` default true) and shared `_shared_fs` (`--config-files` default `/etc/pyrra/*.yaml`, `--prometheus-folder` default `/etc/prometheus/pyrra/`, `--generic-rules` for Grafana). Per-subcommand maps: `api` adds `--prometheus-external-url`/`--grafana-external-url`/`--grafana-external-org-id` (default 1)/`--grafana-external-datasource-id`/`--api-url` (default `http://localhost:9444`)/`--route-prefix`/`--ui-route-prefix`/`--prometheus-bearer-token-path`/`--prometheus-basic-auth-{username,password}`/`--tls-{cert,private-key,client-ca}-file`/`--mimir-org-id`. `kubernetes` adds `--metrics-addr` (default `:8080`)/`--config-map-mode`/`--disable-webhooks` (default true)/`--mimir-url`/`--mimir-prometheus-prefix` (default `prometheus`)/`--mimir-basic-auth-*`/`--mimir-org-id`/`--mimir-write-alerting-rules`/`--mimir-deployment-mode standalone|distributed`/`--enable-leader-election`/`--leader-election-namespace`. `generate` adds `--operator-rule` (generate prometheus-operator `PrometheusRule` files). NOTE: existing `_tracee` already covers all 16 root flags (scope/events/policy/output/artifacts/config/enrichment/signatures-dir/no-signatures/detectors/buffers/stores/server/capabilities/logging/help) — no rewrite needed).
- **retsnoop (libbpf-based return-trace tool) + cilium `features` subcommand fix** (dup-checked clean against `/usr/share/zsh` + `/opt/homebrew/share/zsh` + `/usr/local/share/zsh`) — NEW: `retsnoop` (anakryiko/retsnoop libbpf-based return-trace from src/env.c argp_option table — Andrii Nakryiko's eBPF tool capturing error-return stacks + args of kernel functions; 33 flags grouped via argp into 6 categories (TARGETING/RUNMODE/FILTERING/ADVANCED/CONFIG/HELP). TARGETING: repeatable `*-c/--case bpf|perf` (predefined use cases), repeatable `*-e/--entry GLOB` (error-trigger functions), repeatable `*-a/--allow GLOB`, repeatable `*-d/--deny GLOB`. (`-b/--bootloaders-only`, `-d/--device`, `-l/--list`, `-n/--numeric`, `-t/--timestamp`, `-w/--wait`), doctor (`-y/--yes`/`-n/--no`), mass-compile (`-c/--clean`, `-t/--no-temp`, `-j/--parallel`, `-f/--filter`), docs (`-b/--browser`, `-p/--port`)), `trakt-cli` (angristan/trakt-cli — 3 real subcommands `auth`/`history`/`search` from cmd/{auth,history,search}.go cobra with `--client-id`/`--client-secret` for auth device-code flow, `--type` movies/shows/seasons/episodes filter + `--limit`/`--start-at`/`--end-at` for history, `--type` movie/show/episode/person/list for search; config defaults to `~/.trakt.yaml`), `smithy` (smithy-lang/smithy AWS service-modeling IDL CLI — 12 subcommands `ast`/`build`/`clean`/`diff`/`format`/`init`/`lock`/`migrate`/`select`/`validate`/`version`/`warmup` from smithy-cli/src/main/java/.../commands/*.java with shared `ConfigOptions`/`DiscoveryOptions`/`ValidatorOptions` flag groups: `-c/--config` smithy-build.json + `--no-config`, `--discover`/`--discover-classpath`, `--severity` NOTE/WARNING/DANGER/ERROR + `--no-validate` + `--hide-validators`/`--show-validators` + `--quiet-validation-summary`, plus standard `-q/--quiet`, `--debug`, `--stacktrace`, `--logging` OFF/SEVERE/WARNING/INFO/CONFIG/FINE/FINER/FINEST/ALL, `--no-color`/`--force-color`; per-subcommand maps for build (`--projection`/`--plugin`/`--output`), diff (`--mode` arbitrary/project/git + `--old`/`--new` + `--old-format`/`--new-format`/`--format` text/csv/json + `--events-format`), init (`-l/--list`/`-o/--output`/`-t/--template`/`-u/--url`/`--include-archive`), migrate (`-d/--dry-run`), select (`-e/--expression` selector + `--show-traits` + `--vars`)).

Directory layout:

```
src/              main completions
more_src/         additional completions
man_src/          completions parsed from man pages
override_src/     overrides (prepended to fpath)
architecture_src/ cross-architecture toolchains
```

---

## [0x01] // JACK IN

### Zinit `[RECOMMENDED]`

> `~/.zshrc`

```sh
source "$HOME/.zinit/bin/zinit.zsh"
zinit ice lucid nocompile wait'0e' nocompletions
zinit load MenkeTechnologies/zsh-more-completions
```

> **NOTE:** The `nocompletions` ice prevents zinit from symlinking all completions into `~/.zinit/completions`. Instead the plugin directly manipulates `fpath` — this lets `override_src` completions take priority over defaults while keeping system completions untouched.

### Oh My Zsh

```sh
cd "$HOME/.oh-my-zsh/custom/plugins" && git clone https://github.com/MenkeTechnologies/zsh-more-completions.git
```

Add `zsh-more-completions` to your plugins array in `~/.zshrc`.

OMZ only adds plugin root to fpath, so completions in subdirectories won't load without intervention. You need to wire the nested source dirs into fpath **before** OMZ runs `compinit`:

```sh
# OMZ does not add nested comp dirs to fpath so do it here, assume *src has completions
for plug in ${plugins[@]}; do
    if [[ -d "$ZSH/custom/plugins/$plug" ]]; then
        # null glob - no error
        for dir in "$ZSH/custom/plugins/$plug/"*src(N); do
            if [[ -d "$dir" ]]; then
                if [[ -z ${fpath[(r)$dir]} ]];then
                    if [[ $dir = *override* ]]; then
                        fpath=($dir $fpath)
                    else
                        fpath=($fpath $dir)
                    fi
                fi
            fi
        done
    fi
done
```

### Manual Install

```sh
git clone https://github.com/MenkeTechnologies/zsh-more-completions.git
```

Copy all `_*` files from the source directories to somewhere on your `fpath`.

---

## [0x02] // BOOT SEQUENCE

After install, initialize the completion system:

```sh
autoload -Uz compinit && compinit
```

For faster shell startup, cache the `~/.zcompdump`:

```sh
compinit -C
```

This skips the security check and loads the cached dump directly — **dramatically** faster boot times.

---

## [0x03] // STATS

Counts change constantly; **do not** edit totals by hand. From the repo root:

```sh
zsh scripts/print-repo-stats.zsh
```

This prints `_`-prefixed completion file counts per directory, `total_completions`, and `zunit_tests` (number of `@test` entries under `tests/`).

| Metric | How it is obtained |
|---|---|
| Completion files per dir | `scripts/print-repo-stats.zsh` (uses `find … -name '_*'`) |
| ZUnit tests | `grep '^@test' tests/*.zsh \| wc -l` (same as script output) |
| Generation method | Python scripts parsing `--help` + man pages |
| License | See `license.md` |

---

## [0x04] // TESTING

From the repository root, with [ZUnit](https://github.com/MenkeTechnologies/zunit) on your `PATH`:

```sh
zunit tests/*.zsh
```

GitHub Actions runs the same command on Ubuntu. On macOS, a wrong-case path can still `stat` the file; entries in `tests/t-more-src-existence.zsh` must use the exact basename as on disk (e.g. `_linguist`, not `_Linguist`) so Linux CI passes. `tests/t-repo-invariants.zsh` locks down repo metadata: `blacklist.txt` integrity, `.github/workflows/ci.yml` contract, `license.md`, and absence of tracked `.zwc` files.
